# Changelog ‚Äî 2026-06

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî fix(charly): bundle-node plan steps now run under `charly check live` (the pod path)

A pod bundle's OWN authored plan steps (a bed's `status-shows-pod` check, or any `check:` on the bundle
node) were SILENTLY NOT RUN under `charly check live` ‚Äî `CheckLiveCmd.Run` (the pod path) merged only the
baked candy/box plan + the per-host deploy overlay, never the PROJECT bundle's plan. The VM path
(`loadVmCheckPlans`) and the local path (`runLocalCheck`) already merged it; only the pod path diverged.
The fix mirrors them: the pod check-live composition now also merges `uf.ProjectBundleConfig()`'s bundle
plan (`projectPlan + localPlan`, the per-host overlay replacing by id) into the set. Found during C0 ‚Äî
the `exampleprobe` check had to be baked into the box plan to run on a pod bed; with this fix a
bundle-node check runs too. R10: check-pod runs `status-shows-pod` under check-live (previously absent ‚Äî
check-live went 8‚Üí10 steps, PASS); check-local's `status-shows-local` (the already-correct local path)
confirms no regression.

---

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî refactor(charly): InstallPlan steps ‚Üí provider registry (delete 3 type-switches + dead WalkPlan)

C4 of the plugin program ‚Äî the LAST switch migration: the 3 per-step type-switches (OCI `emitStep` in
build_target_oci.go, local `execStep` in deploy_target_local.go, the VM `emitPlan` loop in
deploy_target_vm.go) are replaced by the provider registry. Each of the 12 InstallStep kinds is a
`StepProvider` (`step_builtins.go`) with `EmitOCI`/`EmitLocal`/`EmitVM` methods preserving their venue's
EXACT prior behaviour cell-by-cell ‚Äî the gate checks (RepoChange hard-errors without
`--allow-repo-changes`; services silent-skip without `--with-services`), the per-VM-cell ReverseOp
collection, and the apk/reboot per-venue skips; the per-target `emitX`/`execX` handlers are unchanged.
The dispatch sites resolve via `providerRegistry.ResolveStep(step.Kind())` and call the matching method;
a bijection (`checkStepProviderBijection`) asserts every kind has a provider. The DEAD, never-wired
`walk_plan.go` (`WalkPlan` + `StepExecutor` ‚Äî a "Phase 1 defined, Phase 2 never done" abstraction
covering only 8 of 12 kinds) is DELETED (R3). Behavior-preserving ‚Äî proven by the full install/emit/
deploy test suite. R5: `git grep 'case *ApkInstallStep:'` / `WalkPlan` / `StepExecutor` ‚Üí only
`CHANGELOG/`. R10: check-pod (OCI emit) + check-k3s-vm (VM emitPlan) + check-local (local execStep),
fresh-rebuild.

---

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî refactor(charly): builders ‚Üí provider registry (delete BuilderImageResolver + 3 builder switches)

C5 of the plugin program: the 3 per-builder switches + the dead injected resolver are replaced by the
provider registry. Each built-in builder (aur/pixi/cargo/npm) is a `BuilderProvider`
(`builder_builtins.go`) carrying its UNCHANGED `Reverse` (teardown ops) + `CollectContext` (per-builder
stage context); `BuilderStep.Reverse` + `collectBuilderContext` resolve via
`providerRegistry.ResolveBuilder`. The aur staging special-case (the `if s.Builder == "aur"` guard in
execBuilder) becomes a `BuilderStager` method (aur ‚Üí `/tmp/aur-pkgs`). The injected
`BuilderImageResolver` func (local + vm targets, the tier-3 fallback) was NEVER wired in production ‚Äî
deleted, leaving the 2-tier override‚Üícompiled-step resolution. A custom candy builder has no provider ‚Üí
falls through (no reverse op, base context only); builders have no CUE vocabulary, so no bijection gate.
Behavior-preserving. R5: `git grep BuilderImageResolver` + the builder `case "aur":` ‚Üí only `CHANGELOG/`.
R10: `install_plan_test` exercises `Reverse` for all 4 builders through the registry (+ aur_replaces_test,
generate_test's OCI aur stage, vm_builder_xhost_test) and check-jupyter-pod builds the
`jupyter-pixi-build` stage (collectBuilderContext + the OCI pixi builder stage) live on a disposable bed.

---

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî refactor(charly): kinds ‚Üí provider registry (delete normalizeNodeInto switch + reservedKindHandlers)

C2 of the plugin program: the per-kind decode dispatch switch in `normalizeNodeInto` is replaced by
the provider registry. Each of the 18 authoring kinds (candy/box/sidecar/distro/builder/init/
resource/agent/group/target/module, the 5 resource-deploy kinds pod/vm/k8s/local/android, and the 2
bundle kinds bundle/host) is a `KindProvider` (`kind_builtins.go`) wrapping its UNCHANGED decode
logic; `normalizeNodeInto` resolves the node's discriminator via `providerRegistry.ResolveKind` and
calls `DecodeNode`. The former `reservedKindHandlers` map (kind‚ÜíCUE-def-path) is folded onto the
providers as `CueDefPath` (R3); `checkKindBijection` ‚Üí `checkKindProviderBijection` (same-init() gate,
run after registration to avoid the alphabetical init-order race). Behavior-preserving ‚Äî proven by
the `*_RoundTrip` tests, which now route through the registry. R5: `git grep reservedKindHandlers` /
`checkKindBijection` ‚Üí only `CHANGELOG/`. R10: box validate (main + box/fedora ‚Äî every entity loads
through the new dispatch) + check-pod (build+load) + check-local (local load).

---

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî refactor(charly): do-mode act dispatch ‚Üí ProvisionActor providers (delete renderProvisionScript)

C1b completes the C1 verb seam: the `renderProvisionScript` switch (the do:act create/configure
renderer for the 7 state-provision verbs file/package/service/user/group/kernel-param/mount) is
replaced by a `ProvisionActor` optional interface on the verb providers. `runProvisionAct` resolves
the verb via `providerRegistry.ResolveVerb` and type-asserts `ProvisionActor`; each renderer is now
a method on its verb provider (`checkrun_act.go`), bodies unchanged. Behavior-preserving. R5:
`git grep renderProvisionScript` ‚Üí only `CHANGELOG/`.

R10: the act path's only LIVE reach is the multi-hour iterate (kind:score) loop ‚Äî `charly check
live` / feature run / `check-pod` set `VerifyOnly`/`SkipDeterministicRun` and skip `run:` steps ‚Äî so
the full act dispatch (resolve ‚Üí ProvisionActor ‚Üí render ‚Üí exec, with pass/fail/skip) is exercised
by a deterministic integration test (`TestRunProvisionActDispatch`, drives the real `runProvisionAct`
through a mock executor; FAILS without C1b). check-pod (fresh-rebuild live bed) confirms the modified
check-runner package integrates and runs end-to-end without regression.

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî refactor(charly): deploy targets ‚Üí provider registry (delete ResolveTarget switch + canonicalTarget)

C3 of the plugin program: `ResolveTarget`'s 5-case dispatch switch + the `canonicalTarget`
legacy-spelling switch are replaced by the provider registry. Each deploy target
(local/vm/pod/k8s/android) is a `DeployTargetProvider` (`deploy_builtins.go`) constructing its
`UnifiedDeployTarget` unchanged; `ResolveTarget` resolves `node.Target` via
`providerRegistry.ResolveDeploy` and calls `ResolveTarget`. The legacy spellings (host‚Üílocal,
container‚Üípod, kubernetes‚Üík8s) become registered aliases (`RegisterBuiltinAlias` + the registry's
alias map); `canonicalDeployWord` normalizes via the resolved provider's `Reserved()`. A
same-init() bijection (`checkDeployProviderBijection`) asserts every canonical target word is a
kind (‚äÜ `spec.KindWords`) AND has a provider. Behavior-preserving. R5: `git grep canonicalTarget`
‚Üí only `CHANGELOG/`. Also corrects a stale C0 comment in `provider_registry.go` (it claimed the
built-in dispatch switches were unmigrated ‚Äî false after C1; R1 documentation-divergence fix).
R10: check-pod (pod target) + check-local (local target).

---

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî refactor(charly): check verbs ‚Üí provider registry (delete the runOne dispatch switch)

C1 of the plugin program: the per-verb runtime DISPATCH switch in `Runner.runOne` is replaced by
the provider registry. Each of the 29 built-in check verbs (file/port/command/http/‚Ä¶ / cdp/wl/dbus/
vnc/mcp/record/spice/libvirt/k8s/adb/appium / summarize/kill / plugin) is a `CheckVerbProvider`
(`verb_builtins.go`) wrapping its UNCHANGED `r.runX` handler; `runOne` resolves the verb via
`providerRegistry.ResolveVerb` and calls `RunVerb`. A new same-init() gate
(`checkVerbProviderBijection`, run after registration to avoid the alphabetical init-order race)
asserts every check-dispatch `spec.OpVerb` has a provider ‚Äî the pure-install verbs
(mkdir/copy/write/link/download/setcap/build) are excluded (they render to install steps, not
checks; `command` is both and stays gated). Behavior-preserving: the live verbs still funnel through
`runCharlyVerb` + the method-allowlist maps. The do-mode act switch (`renderProvisionScript`) and the
validator's per-verb switch (`validate_check.go`) are SEPARATE surfaces, migrated in the C1b
follow-up. R5: `git grep 'dr = r.runCdp'` ‚Üí only `CHANGELOG/`. R10: check-pod (file/port/command/
service/http + the plugin verb) + check-sway-browser-vnc-pod (cdp/wl/vnc/dbus/mcp/record).

---

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî feat(charly): plugin-system foundation ‚Äî ONE unified Provider over the reserved-word registry

First cutover of the plugin program (`~/Atrapub/charly-plugin.md`): a single `Provider`
abstraction keyed by reserved word, generalizing the CUE-single-source reserved-word registry
so every kind/verb (and future deploy/step/builder) is one Provider ‚Äî in-process (built-in) OR
out-of-process (go-plugin gRPC), resolved identically by call sites (transport-invisible).

- **`provider.go` / `provider_registry.go`** ‚Äî the `Provider` interface (`Reserved`/`Class`/
  `Invoke` + the `Operation`/`Result` envelope) and `reservedProviders`, keyed by (class, word)
  because a word like `k8s` is both a kind and a verb. `RegisterBuiltinProvider` (init()) +
  `RegisterPluginProviders` (out-of-proc).
- **The generic `plugin:` check verb** ‚Äî `#OpVerb`/`#Op` gain `plugin`/`plugin_input`; `runOne`
  ‚Üí `runPluginVerb` ‚Üí `providerRegistry.ResolveVerb`. An out-of-tree plugin's verb is authorable
  without recompiling `Op`; an unresolved plugin verb FAILS (never fake-greens).
- **Plugins are candies** ‚Äî `#Candy.plugin:` (`{providers, source}`) + `validatePluginCandy`
  (a builtin provider must be compiled in); a plugin candy needs no install files. The reference
  built-in plugin `candy/plugin-example` provides + tests the `exampleprobe` verb.
- **go-plugin v1.8.0 + grpc v1.61.0 + protobuf** (grpc pinned to go-plugin's k8s-safe minimum ‚Äî
  forcing v1.81.1 downgraded `k8s.io/client-go` to alpha); `charly/plugin/proto` (the uniform
  Invoke envelope, JSON payloads so `spec` stays the single source) + `taskfiles/Proto.yml`
  (checksum-pinned protoc, reproducible); `LocalTransport` + `charly __plugin serve|list`.

Internal dispatch switches (check-verb / kind / deploy / step / builder) migrate in later
cutovers; the out-of-proc git-repo-plugin lifecycle (ExecutorTransport, runtime schema splice,
label discovery) + the bundle-overlay-step-not-running finding are the immediate follow-ups.
R10: check-pod bakes + runs the `exampleprobe` plugin verb on a disposable bed (fresh-rebuild).
Bumps the `box/fedora` gitlink to the matching bed coverage.

---

### 2026-06-21 ‚Äî feat(charly): the init system is a true single-source OCI label (`ai.opencharly.init_def`)

Closes the R3 duplication where the init entrypoint + management commands lived in BOTH the embedded `init:` vocabulary (build-time, but its `entrypoint:`/`fallback_entrypoint:` keys had become DEAD ‚Äî no runtime consumer after the go-quality cutover deleted `initEntrypointArgs`) AND the hardcoded `wellKnownInitDefs` registry (runtime), because the build-time vocab is unavailable at deploy (only the OCI-label init NAME was).

- **New label `ai.opencharly.init_def`** (`labels.go`) carries a dedicated `CapabilityInitDef` JSON subset ‚Äî `entrypoint`, `fallback_entrypoint`, `management_tool`, `management_commands` ‚Äî so build-only `InitDef` fields never leak into the deploy contract. Added per the capabilities recipe: `BoxMetadata.InitDef *CapabilityInitDef` + `CapabilityLabelMap` entry (enforced by `TestCapabilityLabelCompleteness`).
- **Baked at build** in `writeLabels` (`generate.go`) from the vocab-resolved `labelInitDef` (the same `ResolveInitSystem` that already produced `LabelInit`); **read label-first at deploy** ‚Äî `resolveEntrypointFromMeta` (`start.go`) + `resolveInitDefFromMeta` (`service.go`) consult `meta.InitDef` first.
- **`wellKnownInitDefs` retained ONLY as the legacy fallback** for pre-label images (cannot re-bake an already-built image's labels ‚Äî R5 doesn't apply to a still-needed backcompat path); its doc rewritten to say so, and the table frozen (new init systems are declared in the vocab, not added here).
- **Capability win:** the dead vocab `entrypoint:`/`fallback_entrypoint:`/`management_*` keys are now LIVE (consumed ‚Üí label), and **custom init systems declared only in the vocab now work at RUNTIME** (their full contract travels in the label ‚Äî previously "build-only"). The stale "honored at build only" comments + skill notes are corrected.

Runtime class: `golangci-lint` 0, `go build/vet/test` (5 new tests: round-trip, legacy-fallback for supervisord+systemd, custom-init-at-runtime, capability completeness), `task cue:gen` reproducible, `charly box validate`. R8: a freshly-built supervisord image carries the label (`charly box labels ‚Ä¶ --format ai.opencharly.init_def` ‚Üí the resolved entrypoint + management commands) and the deployed quadlet's `Exec=supervisord -n -c /etc/supervisord.conf` derives from it. R10: the `check-pod` disposable bed end-to-end (`PASS`, 10 steps incl. fresh-rebuild; host clean). Bumps the `plugins` gitlink to the matching skill updates.

---

### 2026-06-20 ‚Äî chore(charly): go-quality cleanup ‚Äî golangci-lint to zero + gofmt

Resolved the full charly Go-quality backlog (the go-quality skill's 1017-issue baseline is STALE ‚Äî the real audit was 13 `golangci-lint` findings + 9 `gofmt` files; the tree has been heavily cleaned since, partly by the CUE-single-source cutover deleting offending code). All fixed MANUALLY (never `golangci-lint --fix` ‚Äî it corrupts this tree) with adversarial default-refute triage:

- **5 staticcheck `QF1012`** (`internal/schemagen`) ‚Üí `fmt.Fprintf` (proven output-stable by `TestGenReproducible`).
- **4 `unconvert`** (`config.go` √ó3, `intermediates.go`) ‚Äî redundant `[]string(...)` on fields already `[]string` (the generated `spec.Box.Build`).
- **1 `unparam` `specSource`** ‚Äî dropped the never-used `[]string` return (both callers discarded it).
- **1 `unparam` `builderPhaseTemplate`** (phase always `PhaseInstall`) ‚Üí `//nolint:unparam` (reasoned): it's the uniform-signature `BuilderDef` analog of `formatPhaseTemplate` (which DOES vary phase via `s.Phase`); the three-phase machinery is documented forward design (`install_build.go:505`), no builder authors `prepare:`/`cleanup:` yet ‚Äî removing the param would delete reachable schema-backed generality.
- **1 `gocyclo` `(*Op).VerbsSet`** (47) ‚Üí `//nolint:gocyclo` (reasoned): the skill's exact flat exactly-one-verb enumeration archetype; extraction would relocate cases without clarifying.
- **1 `unused` `initEntrypointArgs`** ‚Üí DELETED. RCA (skill: an unused unexported func may be a latent missing-caller bug): `git log --all -S "EntrypointArgs("` proves `InitDef.EntrypointArgs` was NEVER wired in any commit (the CUE cutover free-func'd an already-dead method); the runtime entrypoint resolves exclusively from the separate hardcoded `wellKnownInitDefs` registry (`service.go:131`), so the func is unreachable by construction ‚Äî genuinely dead, not a regression.
- **`gofmt -w`** on 9 files (7 test files + `schemagen/main.go` + `spec/hand_state_types.go`) ‚Äî AST-identical.

Gate: `golangci-lint run ./...` = **0 issues**, `gofmt -l .` empty, `go build/vet/test` green, `TestGenReproducible` (pinned cue v0.16.1) byte-identical, `charly box validate`, and the `check-pod` disposable bed end-to-end (`PASS`, 10 steps incl. fresh-rebuild; host clean). No `plugins` change. Candidate follow-up surfaced (non-blocking): the embedded vocab's init `entrypoint:`/`fallback_entrypoint:` keys now have no Go consumer (they were already dead) ‚Äî delete or annotate in a later cutover.

### 2026-06-20 ‚Äî fix(charly): deploy-config state correctness ‚Äî idempotent migrate of a kind-named node + VM-bed entry teardown

Two deploy-config state-handling bugs the prior cutover's R10 surfaced (no authored format change ‚Üí no schema bump):

- **`migrate --dry-run` perpetually (wrongly) reported `would apply unified-node`** on the repo's own root `charly.yml`. RCA: the repo has a node-form entity literally NAMED `vm` (`vm: {vm: {source: ‚Ä¶}}` ‚Äî a valid node-form VM entity whose name collides with the `vm` kind keyword), and `migrateUnifiedNodeDoc` keyed on `legacyKindMapKeys["vm"]` and re-ran the legacy-kind-map rewrite path on it, rebuilding to byte-identical output but returning `changed=true`. Fix (`migrate_unified_node.go`): skip a top-level kind-word entry whose value is ALREADY node-form ‚Äî `!legacyKindMapKeys[k] || (nodeShapedValue(v) && !mapHasKey(v,"name"))`. A genuine legacy collection (`vm: {arch: ‚Ä¶, cachyos: ‚Ä¶}`, entity-name children) is not `nodeShapedValue` and still converts; a legacy single-entity (`vm: {name: ‚Ä¶}`) keeps its `name:` key and still converts. `charly migrate --dry-run` from the repo root now reports `nothing to migrate`.
- **`removeVmDeployEntry` leaked a stale bundle entry** for a `kind: check` VM bed. RCA: a check-VM bed (`check-k3s-vm`) WRITES its `vm_state` under the BUNDLE key (`check-k3s-vm`), but every teardown caller REMOVES the prefixed VM-entity key (`vm:k3s-vm`) ‚Äî an exact-key lookup that missed, so the domain was destroyed but the config entry leaked (and the entry carried no `vm:` cross-ref to resolve it back). Fix (`bundle_add_cmd_vm.go`): `saveVmDeployState` gains a `vmEntity` param and persists `entry.Vm` (the cross-ref linkage); `removeVmDeployEntry` resolves the actual written key(s) via `vmDeployEntryKeys` ‚Äî the literal name AND every bundle whose `vm:` cross-ref names the entity ‚Äî with no over-match.

Runtime class: `go test ./...` (3 new tests incl. node-named-`vm` idempotency, legacy-collection-still-converts, bundle-keyed-entry-removal), `task cue:gen` reproducible, `charly box validate`, repo-root `migrate --dry-run` clean, and the `check-k3s-vm` disposable VM bed end-to-end (`PASS`, 6 phases incl. fresh-rebuild + full k3s suite; **post-teardown the host config has zero `check-k3s-vm` entries** and the fix also cleaned the pre-existing leaked entry; no orphan domain; 8 unrelated entries survived). No `plugins` change.

---

### 2026-06-20 ‚Äî fix(charly): harden the per-host migrate path ‚Äî empty-dir relocate orphan, testdata skip, vm-state write lock, `ov_install_strategy` key

Follow-up to the CUE-single-source cutover: five per-host migrate-path residuals the R10 bed gate surfaced (none changed an authored wire key).

- **Empty-`~/.config/charly`-dir relocate orphan** (`migrate_charly_rebrand.go`): `relocateHostStateForCharly` retargeted `ctx.HostDeployPath` onto `~/.config/charly` even when the `~/.config/ov ‚Üí ~/.config/charly` move was SKIPPED because `~/.config/charly` already existed (empty), orphaning the real overlay at `~/.config/ov/deploy.yml` and no-op'ing the chain on a phantom path (`charly migrate` silently recovered nothing). New `mergeHostStateDir(from,to)` moves every non-conflicting top-level entry into the empty/lacking target (NEVER clobbering a pre-existing entry) then removes the emptied source ‚Äî so a host in that state recovers with no manual `rmdir`.
- **Migrate walked `charly/testdata`** (non-idempotent dev-repo noise): R3-unified the two duplicated candidate scanners into one `migrateCandidateYAMLFiles` (`migrate_walk.go`) that skips any `testdata` path component (alongside the existing nested-submodule skip); `opUnifyCandidateFiles` + `dropBoxPortCandidateFiles` now delegate to it. ALL doc-migration steps honor the skip (197 candidates, 0 testdata).
- **`saveVmDeployState` lost-update race** (`bundle_add_cmd_vm.go`): the VM-state read-modify-write now takes the same blocking `acquireDeployConfigLock` `saveDeployState`/`cleanDeployEntry` use (applied to `removeVmDeployEntry` too); reentrancy-audited ‚Äî no caller holds the lock, so no self-deadlock (flock per-open-fd).
- **`ov_install_strategy` ‚Üí `charly_install_strategy`** vm_state key (`migrate_install_strategy_key.go`): new `install-strategy-key` migration step at intra-HEAD CalVer `2026.169.0002` (between `unified-node` and `step-venue`) renames the key at every depth on project files AND the per-host overlay; a reflection test pins the rename target to the live `spec.VmDeployState` yaml tag. NO `LatestSchemaVersion` bump ‚Äî this COMPLETES the already-landed 2026.159 ov‚Üícharly rebrand's coverage of an internal deploy-state key, not a new format (HEAD stays `2026.169.0004`; a HEAD bump was empirically proven wrong ‚Äî it breaks `box validate` on the superproject + 5 box submodules already at HEAD).

Runtime class: `go test ./...` (8 new tests incl. concurrent-writers-all-survive, orphan-recovery, testdata-skip, key-rename + struct-tag pin), `task cue:gen` reproducible, `charly box validate`, and the `check-k3s-vm` disposable VM bed end-to-end (`PASS (steps=6)`, the now-locked `persist-auto-port` allocating + persisting + reusing SSH port 44949 with no self-deadlock; host clean after, no orphan domain). Bumps the `plugins` gitlink to the matching migrate-skill note. Two orthogonal pre-existing issues were observed and left for a separate cutover (a `migrateUnifiedNodeDoc` root-`charly.yml` dry-run non-idempotency present on `main`; `removeVmDeployEntry` targeting the `vm:` key not a bundle key).

---

### 2026-06-20 ‚Äî refactor(charly): CUE `schema/*.cue` is the single source of truth ‚Äî Go param structs + reserved-word vocabulary are GENERATED (gengotypes reversal)

**`charly/schema/*.cue` is now the SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH for the `charly.yml` ingress grammar.** The Go param structs, the reserved-word vocabulary, and the kind/verb wiring are GENERATED or DERIVED from the CUE defs ‚Äî there are no hand-maintained parallel copies. `task cue:gen` regenerates the new `charly/spec` package from `charly/schema/*.cue`; `charly/spec/cue_types_gen.go` is emitted by **`cue exp gengotypes`** (then yaml-retagged), and `charly/spec_aliases.go` repoints every package-main param type to its generated twin via `type X = spec.X` (`BoxConfig`, `Op`, `CandyYAML`, `VmSpec`, `ServiceEntry`, ‚Ä¶) so the **Go compiler itself is the field-parity check** ‚Äî a renamed or dropped spec field fails the build at that surface.

**The long-standing do-NOT-use-`gengotypes` guidance is REVERSED.** The former `/charly-internals:go` point-5 rule ("Do NOT generate the Go structs with `cue exp gengotypes` ‚Äî it generalizes disjunctions to `any` and remaps names; keep the hand lockstep instead") no longer holds. The precision loss is handled at the source: every lossy CUE disjunction is annotated `@go(-)` to suppress its generated type, and the faithful Go union/shorthand/state type is hand-written in the SAME `spec` package (`spec/union_types.go`, `spec/scalar_aliases.go`, `spec/hand_state_types.go`) and referenced by name. The committed generated Go can never drift from the schema ‚Äî `charly/spec/gen_repro_test.go` re-runs the exact `task cue:gen` toolchain into a temp dir and diffs against the committed `cue_types_gen.go` + `vocab_gen.go` (skipping gracefully when the pinned `cue` CLI is absent).

**The reserved-word vocabulary + per-verb method allowlists are DERIVED from CUE, and the eight hand vocab lists are DELETED.** `charly/spec/vocab_gen.go` (emitted by the companion generator `charly/internal/schemagen` `-mode=vocab`, via the embedded `cuelang.org/go` API) carries the single-source slices ‚Äî `KindWords`, `ResourceKinds`, `DocDirectives`, `StepKeywords`, `ContextWords`, `DataKeys`, `OpFields`, `OpVerbs`, `AuthoringVerbs`, and the `LiveVerbMethods` allowlist map. The eight hand-maintained lists that previously hard-coded the same words are gone ‚Äî `kindKeys`/`kindKeysSet`, `rootShapeKeys`, `docDirectiveKeys` (`unified.go`) and `nodeEntityKinds`, `nodeResourceKinds`, `nodeStepVerbs`, `nodeDataKeys`, `nodeDocDirectives` (`node_parse.go`) ‚Äî replaced by `kindWordSet` / `resourceKindSet` / `stepKeywordSet` / `dataKeySet` / `docDirectiveSet` set-views in `reserved_registry.go`. The schema concatenation is unified in the new leaf package `charly/internal/schemaconcat`: ONE `ConcatSchema` that both the runtime (`cue_schema.go`'s `sharedCueSchema`) and the dev-time generator call, so the validated schema and the generated types can never diverge.

**A reserved-word‚Üíhandler registry + a startup bijection gate enforce that every kind/verb is wired.** `charly/reserved_registry.go` binds each kind word to its CUE def (`"vm" ‚Üí "#Vm"`), each verb to its `VerbCatalog` entry, and each live-verb method to its `liveVerbDispatch` handler; its `init()` runs three bijection checks fail-fast at process start (mirrored as `TestReservedWordRegistry_{KindBijection,VerbBijection,MethodAllowlists,KindsDispatchable}` in `reserved_registry_test.go`) ‚Äî `checkKindBijection`, `checkVerbBijection`, `checkMethodAllowlists` ‚Äî so a kind/verb/method can no longer be added to the schema without a handler, nor a handler survive its word's deletion.

**`#NodeDoc` is the sole load-time grammar gate; the legacy kind-keyed/root-shape routing and `keylint.go` are DELETED.** `mergeUnifiedDocs` runs every document ‚Äî root `charly.yml` and discovered manifests alike ‚Äî through `classifyDoc` ‚Üí the closed `#NodeDoc` CUE gate ‚Üí `normalizeNodeInto`; a legacy kind-keyed / root-shape document is no longer routed but HARD-REJECTED with a `charly migrate` hint (the `mergeKindDoc` / `firstKindKey` / `VmDoc` routing is removed). The whole `keylint.go` / `keylint_test.go` yaml.v3 `KnownFields` unknown-key linter is deleted ‚Äî CUE's closed-schema check is the real unknown-key gate now, so its self-decoding-types carve-out is gone too. Also deleted: the orphaned `group_spec.go`, `module_spec.go`, `resource_config.go`, `target_spec.go` hand structs the generated `spec` package supersedes.

**No authored wire key changed ‚Äî there is NO schema-version bump and NO `charly migrate` step.** This cutover replaces HOW the grammar is sourced (hand structs + hand vocab lists ‚Üí generated-from-CUE), not the grammar itself: every `charly.yml` that loaded before loads identically after, and the "legacy forms hard-rejected" above are the pre-existing pre-`#NodeDoc` shapes already gated by the unified-node migration, not a new wire change. `LatestSchemaVersion()` stays **`2026.169.0004`** and the migration registry is untouched. Runtime class: `go test ./...` (the `gen_repro` reproducibility gate, the `reserved_registry` bijection gates, the CUE corpus + closedness tests), `task cue:gen` reproducing the committed `spec` package, and `charly box validate` across the superproject + every `box/<distro>` submodule. Bumps the `plugins` gitlink to the matching skill sweep.

### 2026-06-20 ‚Äî fix(chrome-cdp): forward caller flags via "$@" so Chrome's welcome dialog is suppressed and it starts maximized (`v2026.171.0416`)

The `chrome-wrapper` exec block lacked `"$@"`, so the launch flags the supervised `[program:chrome]` service (`selkies-core`) and `chrome-restart` passed were silently DROPPED ‚Äî on the selkies streaming desktops Chrome showed its first-run "welcome / make default" dialog and opened un-maximized. Fix: the launch flags now live in the wrapper itself (single source) and `"$@"` forwards any caller flags; `chrome-restart` and the `selkies-core` chrome service are simplified to call the bare wrapper. The old callers' `--force-renderer-accessibility` (inert under the dropped-flags bug, so production Chrome never actually had it) is intentionally NOT restored ‚Äî CDP automation does not need forced renderer a11y. Adds 3 deterministic `selkies-core` checks that FAIL without the fix: `selkies-core-chrome-launch-flags` (`--no-first-run` + `--start-maximized` in the live `/proc/<pid>/cmdline`), `selkies-core-chrome-maximized` (CDP-measured window ‚âà screen ‚Üí `MAXOK`, proving maximize took effect not merely the flag), `selkies-core-frame-not-uniform` (real composited frame, not a black void ‚Äî closes the same false-green gap the `agent-check` leaves under `--no-agent`). Verified on the `check-selkies-labwc-pod` bed (180 steps, 0 failed; all 3 new checks PASS on a fresh rebuild) + a live screenshot of the maximized welcome-free Chrome. The selkies-KDE flavor has a separate no-systemd-user session instability that blocks ITS bed (HELD as a dedicated effort ‚Äî see the `selkies-kde-kwin-instability` memory: systemd1 `/bin/false` storm + wl-paste/wlr-data-control leak both fixed there, chrome CDP `unix_wait_for_peer` needs a real systemd-user); this fix is the shared chrome candy, proven on the labwc flavor. candy `chrome-cdp` ‚Üí 2026.170.2101, `selkies-core` ‚Üí 2026.170.2327.

### 2026-06-19 ‚Äî feat(charly)!: unified name-first node model for all of charly.yml + GPU auto-preemptible arbitration (`v2026.170.1105`)

charly.yml collapses to ONE name-first node model ‚Äî every entity, bundle member,
plan step, and data field is a `<name>: {<kind>: ‚Ä¶, <child-nodes>}` node, one
`#Node` CUE schema at every depth (CLOSED, fully validated before anything
executes). `deploy:`‚Üí`bundle:`, `charly deploy`‚Üí`charly bundle`,
`DeploymentNode`‚Üí`BundleNode`. Venue + membership now come from TREE POSITION ‚Äî
the authored `on:`/`pod:`(step)/`peer:`/`nested:`/`target:` keys are REMOVED; a
step nested under a member runs on that member, a resource node placed under
another deploys into it. `${HOST:<member>}` (`:<port>` for a host-reachable
endpoint) is the SOLE cross-member address, superseding
`${PEER_HOST}`/`${PEER_ENDPOINT}`. A new `agent_provisioned: true` tree-child flag
marks agent-built bed pods (foldMembers skips them ‚Äî the iterate-benchmark
contract). An idempotent `charly migrate` step (+ registry HEAD bump) synthesizes
all of it from any legacy config. CUE stays the closed schema authority.

GPU resource-arbitration robustness: a pod that USES the nvidia GPU device
auto-claims `requires_shared:[nvidia-gpu]` (`acquireResourceForClaimant` ‚Üí
`withImpliedGPUShared`), so EVERY GPU consumer is a tracked, preemptable shared
claimant with no per-deploy config ‚Äî the `requires_exclusive:` arbiter then
gracefully preempts them and flips nvidia‚Üívfio fully automatically. The switch's
EBUSY refusal now NAMES the external holder (`formatNvidiaHolders` /
`discoverNvidiaHolders`) instead of a cryptic message.

R10 (fresh rebuild, RTX 4080): `check-cross-pod-cdp` PASS; `check-selkies-kde-nvidia-vm`
from-box nested-pod deploy + nvidia‚Üívfio switch + in-guest GPU live-proven; a
`gpu-holder` ordinary pod auto-claimed + preempted on-card; full bed roster (24
beds + 3 cross beds) proven on the unified loader; `charly box validate` exit 0
across all 6 repos; `go test`/`golangci` green. Known immediate-next cutovers:
box-submodule candy `@github` pins ‚Üí `charly box reconcile` to this tag; the
selkies-kde desktop stream (:3000) needs GSettings schemas + an
xdg-desktop-portal rootless-fuse fix (a selkies-kde candy issue, not this change).

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî chore(hooks): end-of-turn reminder gains an autonomy anchor (`v2026.168.1602`)

`end-of-turn-challenge.sh` (the `Stop` hook) was rewritten to emphasize
autonomous completion: if ANY cutover / task / TODO is still unfinished the
answer to "should I continue?" is ALWAYS YES ‚Äî keep going automatically (Hard
Cutover runs end-to-end through R10; disposable:true targets need no extra
permission), never stopping merely to ask whether to proceed; EVERY failure /
warning / anomaly must get a proper RCA + real fix per CLAUDE.md (R1), with
"flake" / "transient" / "out of scope" / "follow-up" forbidden (R2); and the hook
STOPs only when all work is done AND verified, or when a genuine, unresolvable
question blocks (then ONE specific question). Still soft (exit 0) and
pointer-shaped ‚Äî no rule bodies restated. The `/charly-internals:agents` Hooks
doctrine row summarizes the hook's re-audit role and stays accurate (the autonomy
anchor is a behavioral anchor it does not enumerate). Hook-script change class.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî docs+chore(changelog,hooks): per-repo monthly `CHANGELOG/` + full-roster compliance reminder + deterministic CHANGELOG gate (`v2026.168.1551`)

History moved from a single ever-growing root `CHANGELOG.md` to a per-repo
`CHANGELOG/` directory with one file per calendar month (`YYYY-MM.md`). The
7937-line root monolith was split along its existing `## YYYY-MM` markers into
`CHANGELOG/{2026-06,2026-05,2026-04}.md` (all 221 dated monthly entries preserved
verbatim); its 3 trailing non-month thematic sections (engineering cautionary
tales, early schema cutovers, relocated layer/image/command history) were dropped
as outdated; the monolith was deleted (hard cutover). Every repository in the project ‚Äî superproject, `plugins`,
`pkg/{arch,fedora,debian}`, `box/{arch,cachyos,debian,fedora,ubuntu}` ‚Äî now keeps
its **own** `CHANGELOG/` (each seeded with a `README.md` index + this month's
file); history is repo-scoped, never centralized.

The two soft compliance hooks were strengthened to drive a SECOND-PASS
verification (operator: "a REMINDER not a full duplication"):
`runtime-verification-reminder.sh` now names the full R0‚ÄìR10 + RDD + ADE roster
as terse second-pass *triggers* (pointers to CLAUDE.md, never rule-body copies),
and `end-of-turn-challenge.sh` now prompts a re-audit of every code/config change
against R0‚ÄìR10 + the Acceptance checklist and a check that each changed repo
recorded its current-month `CHANGELOG/` entry. `pre-commit-gate.sh` gains a
deterministic gate: a runtime-tier commit (`fully tested and validated` /
`analysed on a live system`) in a repo that tracks `CHANGELOG/` must stage a
`CHANGELOG/YYYY-MM.md` entry ‚Äî pure submodule-pointer-bump commits and
documentation-tier commits are exempt; the `DOC_PATH` docs-classifier is
unchanged (a `CHANGELOG/YYYY-MM.md` path already matches its `.md` clause). The
"Hooks doctrine" was amended to bless the fuller pointer roster (the quantitative
"‚â§10 lines / one behavioral anchor" caps are lifted) while keeping its
anti-duplication core ‚Äî hooks still never restate rule *bodies*; CLAUDE.md
remains the single source. Doc-only across `*.md` + the three hook scripts (the
hook-script change class); the new gate self-verified the superproject commit.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(selkies-kde): KWin wl-probes source the live compositor env (`eval`, not `check`) (`v2026.168.1408`)

The selkies-kde streaming desktop's `charly check wl` probes
(`kde-wl-keyboard-wtype`, `kde-wl-toplevel-via-kdotool`) failed on the KWin
session: `wtype` reported "Compositor does not support the virtual keyboard
protocol" and `kdotool` reported "org.kde.KWin was not provided".

Root cause: `wlCompositorEnvPrelude` (wl.go) is designed to source the running
compositor's live `WAYLAND_DISPLAY` + `DBUS_SESSION_BUS_ADDRESS` from
`/proc/<pid>/environ` ‚Äî KWin (started via `startplasma-wayland` under
`dbus-run-session`) renders into `wayland-1` (pixelflux) and registers
`org.kde.KWin` on a RANDOM `/tmp/dbus-XXXXXX` bus, not the baked defaults. But the
prelude applied the sourced exports with `check "$(...)"` instead of
`eval "$(...)"`; `check` is not a command, so the exports silently dropped and the
probe fell back to `wayland-0` + the baked `/tmp/dbus-session`, where wtype's
virtual-keyboard protocol is absent and `org.kde.KWin` is unregistered. One
`check`->`eval` typo broke BOTH the keyboard and the window probes at once.

Fix: `check`->`eval` in `wlCompositorEnvPrelude`. RDD-proven on a live selkies-kde
pod (wtype "Typed 6 characters"; kdotool listed the live KWin windows). The
kde-selkies supervisorctl-status check is marked `context: runtime` to match its
sibling (supervisord runs only in a live deploy). R5 claim-keyed sweep: the same
`eval`->`check` corruption in the secrets / direnv / charly-config / layer
SKILL.md `.envrc` / `.secrets` / direnv-hook examples was fixed in the plugins
repo (documentation reviewed).

R10: `check-selkies-kde-pod` PASS (10 steps; the 5 `kde-wl-*` probes green)
through the fresh-rebuild gate, run three times. Regression guard in
`wl_kwin_test.go` asserts the prelude sources via `eval` and never `check`.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(check): committed-APK checks anchor to the authoring candy ‚Äî fail hard, no fallback (`v2026.168.1403`)

The android-emulator-pod bed's `adb: install` / `appium: install-app` checks
(android-emulator-layer's `apk: ./tests/data/ApiDemos-debug.apk`) resolved the
fixture cwd-relative and died with `open ./tests/data/...: no such file` ‚Äî only
under a `box/<distro>` bed run, never in the unit tests (which passed the Origin
in by hand).

Two root causes, both masked by a silent cwd-relative fall-through in
`resolveCheckApk` (and by an override-fallback patch that, it turned out, never
even executed for this bug ‚Äî `resolveCheckApk` returned on the empty-origin guard
long before reaching it):

1. **The per-step `Op.Origin` was never stamped.** The authoring candy's origin
   lives ONCE on the baked `LabeledDescription` group, not per-step in the OCI
   label; `RunPlan`/`runUnit` dispatched each step's `Op` without re-stamping
   `op.Origin = fs.origin`, so `resolveCheckApk` saw an empty `c.Origin` and could
   not key `CandyDirs`.
2. **`charly check feature run` never populated `CandyDirs`.** Only `charly check
   live` built the candy‚Üísource-dir map, so the same committed-APK check passed
   under check-live yet failed (`0 candies scanned`) under feature-run ‚Äî cascading
   into 36 downstream appium failures against a then-absent ApiDemos.

Fix ‚Äî fail hard, no obfuscating fallback:

- `description_run.go`: stamp `op.Origin = fs.origin` onto every dispatched `Op`.
- `check_cmd.go`: a shared `attachCheckRunnerContext` helper wires identity +
  `CandyDirs` for BOTH `charly check live` AND `charly check feature run`, so the
  two can never diverge again (R3 ‚Äî one anchoring path).
- `resolveApkPath` / `resolveCheckApk` / `candySourceDirs` now return errors and
  FAIL HARD on any unanchorable committed APK (non-candy origin, absent
  `CandyDirs` entry, candy-scan error, file missing under the candy tree) ‚Äî no
  silent cwd-relative pass-through, no `CHARLY_REPO_OVERRIDE` fallback.

R10: `check-android-emulator-pod` PASS (15/15 steps) through the fresh-rebuild
gate (feature-run 260 passed / 0 failed / 20 skipped); `check-selkies-kde-pod`
PASS (shared-runner regression check). Regression guard
`TestRunPlan_StampsStepOrigin` fails without the origin stamp.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(candy): unsloth-studio installs the Studio CLI via the official installer (`v2026.168.1135`)

The supervised `unsloth studio` service FATAL'd "can't find command 'unsloth'":
the prior fix wrongly assumed the `unsloth` pip package ships the Studio CLI ‚Äî it
ships the FastLanguageModel fine-tuning LIBRARY. Per upstream the CLI comes from
the curl installer. Added a build-time `curl -fsSL https://unsloth.ai/install.sh |
sh` run step (self-installs uv, lands `~/.local/bin/unsloth`, bootstraps the
`~/.unsloth/studio` venv at build so the supervised launch is immediate) with a
`test -x` build-time guard; `distro.arch.package: cmake + git + base-devel` (the
installer builds its GGUF engine from source and on Arch does not auto-install
them); the service execs the launcher by absolute path. R10:
`check-cachyos-unsloth-studio-pod` PASS (10 steps, 85 check-live, 0 failed) through
the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(candy): java-openjdk resolves /usr/bin/java on Arch (`v2026.168.1031`)

On Arch/CachyOS `/usr/bin/java` symlinks through `/usr/lib/jvm/default-runtime`,
which ships UNSET (-> `/dev/null`) until `archlinux-java set` runs, so the absolute
launcher failed with ENOTDIR. Added a guarded `archlinux-java set` (a no-op on
Fedora/Debian/Ubuntu, which wire update-alternatives at install) pointing the
system default at JDK 21, and cleaned a malformed run-step whose prose leaked a
`command=...` body. analysed on a live system: `check-android-emulator-pod`
(cachyos) built fresh and ran check-image + check-live ‚Äî all java-openjdk checks
PASS; the bed's full gate did not complete due to the then-unfixed committed-APK
fixture-path bug (its own cutover, since landed as `v2026.168.1403`).

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(candy): redis-responds probe is host-independent (`v2026.168.0957`)

The `redis-responds` check ran `redis-cli` from the HOST against
`${HOST_PORT:6379}`; on a multi-service pod where the host port mapping is not
under test this is fragile. Probe redis INSIDE the container on its fixed port 6379
(`in_container: true`), proving the supervised `redis-server` answers regardless of
host remapping; the separate `redis-port-open` check still proves host TCP
reachability. R10: `check-cachyos-immich-ml-pod` PASS (10 steps, 128 check-live, 0
failed) through the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(candy): chrome/direnv/thunar check correctness (`v2026.168.0944`)

chrome: removed the `google-chrome-stable --version` check ‚Äî RDD on a live pod
proved that when chrome-cdp wraps the binary, `--version` LAUNCHES a full browser
and hangs ~125s, driving every desktop bed's check-live to the readiness cap; the
file/package/`.desktop` checks already prove chrome is installed. direnv: the
`/etc/profile.d/charly-direnv-<shell>.sh` drop-in said `check "$(direnv hook X)"` ‚Äî
`check` is no builtin, so direnv was never hooked and every login shell printed
"check: command not found"; fixed to `eval`, with discriminating checks. thunar:
`package_map {fedora: Thunar}` (the Fedora rpm capitalizes the name). R10:
`check-sway-browser-vnc-pod` PASS (10 steps; check-live 34s vs the prior 30-min
cap-kill) through the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(candy): cross-distro nested-container + gocryptfs/supervisord robustness (`v2026.168.0927`)

container-nesting on Debian/Ubuntu: add `libcap2-bin` (provides `setcap(8)`, which
Fedora/Arch ship transitively but Debian/Ubuntu do not ‚Äî without it the setcap RUN
step exits 127 and fails the build); `chmod u-s` newuidmap/newgidmap (Debian/Ubuntu
ship them setuid-root, which fails in a nested rootless userns when combined with
file capabilities ‚Äî match Fedora/Arch's cap-only posture); resolve the uid-1000
user via getent. gocryptfs: widen the version-banner regex (newer gocryptfs drops
the leading `v`). supervisord: accept `XDG_RUNTIME_DIR` = `/tmp/xdg-runtime` OR
`/tmp` and test by exit status. R10: PASS on `check-fedora-coder-pod` (278),
`check-charly-fedora-pod` (106), `check-debian-coder-pod` (272),
`check-ubuntu-coder-pod` (272) through the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(check): load-robust check-live ‚Äî per-probe never-hang + generous PollHeavy bound (`v2026.168.0829`)

Under heavy parallel load a slow-but-progressing `charly check live` pass was
SIGKILLed: `stepReady` ran the WHOLE multi-probe pass under a 120s `PerAttempt` and
the probes shared one ctx with no per-probe bound, so a 100+-probe pass needing
>120s was killed every tick to the 30-min cap (bed FAIL, empty step log). Fix: a
per-probe never-hang (each probe attempt under
`context.WithTimeout(ctx, probeNeverHang)`, honoring a longer author `timeout:`) so
a wedged probe is cancelled individually and the pass continues; and PollHeavy now
uses a new `PerAttemptHeavy` (15m default; config + env + closed `#Readiness`
schema) so the whole subprocess is never guillotined mid-pass. R10:
`check-fedora-coder-pod` (278 steps) under load avg ~30 PASS ‚Äî check-live 217s,
feature-run 215s, feature-run-rebuild 219s (all >120s); new tests fail when the fix
is neutralized.

### 2026-06-17 ‚Äî fix(gpu)!: device_lock-safe group-aware GPU driver switch + wedge poisoning + `charly vm gpu recover` (`v2026.168.0526`)

Root-caused and fixed the GPU driver-switch wedge that, in the prior campaign,
hung the host's nvidia card uninterruptibly and required a reboot.

**Root cause (source-confirmed against NVIDIA's open kernel modules
`kernel-open/nvidia/nv-pci.c`, then RDD-proven on the live RTX 4080 SUPER).** A
sysfs `unbind` of the `nvidia` driver fires `nv_pci_remove ‚Üí
nv_pci_remove_helper(block_if_gpu_in_use=TRUE)`, which ‚Äî when `nvl->usage_count
!= 0` (any open `/dev/nvidia*` fd, live CUDA context, or
`nvidia_uvm`/`nvidia_modeset`/`nvidia_drm` still attached) ‚Äî blocks forever in
`while (usage_count != 0) os_delay(500)`. The Linux PCI core holds the
per-device `device_lock` (`dev->mutex`, uninterruptible) across the entire
`.remove`, so every later bind/reset/remove on the device serializes behind it
in unkillable `D` state. Recovery is reboot-only: no userspace primitive
releases a held `device_lock`. It is **not** power/runtime-PM related (a
disproven earlier hypothesis); `nv_pci_shutdown` passes `block=FALSE` so host
reboot/shutdown never wedges.

**The fix (prevention + cascade containment, not avoidance):**
- `charly/gpu_driver_switch.go` rewritten ‚Äî the switch is now **group-aware**
  (flips EVERY function of the IOMMU group: display‚Üínvidia/vfio,
  HDMI-audio‚Üísnd_hda_intel/vfio; a VFIO group is guest-usable only when all
  members are vfio-bound) and the nvidia‚Üívfio detach uses **`modprobe -r`**
  (module-refcount-guarded ‚Üí `EBUSY` fast-fail if a client holds the GPU; it can
  never reach the blocking `.remove` loop) ‚Äî it NEVER sysfs-unbinds a busy
  nvidia. `runGPUSwitchScript` is bounded (context deadline + `WaitDelay`) so a
  GSP-teardown stall frees charly + the arbiter lock instead of blocking forever;
  a confirmed wedge returns the new `errGPUSwitchWedged` sentinel.
- `charly/preempt.go` ‚Äî on a wedge the arbiter **POISONS** the GPU resource
  (a boot-id-keyed marker under the preemption dir) and refuses it to every later
  claimant, including `reconcileStranded`, so a wedged card can never be handed
  out to produce a second `D`-state; the poison clears on reboot.
- `charly/vm_gpu_cmd.go` ‚Äî `charly vm gpu status` now reports **per-function**
  driver + IOMMU group + mode and flags a wedged/poisoned card; new `charly vm
  gpu recover` rebinds an unbound/half-switched card to vfio-pci but, on a true
  wedge, reports reboot-required and attempts nothing (a bind would re-wedge).
  `charly vm gpu mode` switches the whole group.

**Removed (R5 claim-keyed sweep).** The load-bearing comment in
`gpu_driver_switch.go` asserting "Only the DISPLAY function is ever flipped; the
sibling AUDIO function stays on vfio-pci ‚Ä¶ RDD-proven" is DELETED ‚Äî it was false
(the real constraint is IOMMU-group VFIO viability, and the wedge was never
about module liveness). The vfio/GPU model in `/charly-vm:vm` (new "GPU
driver-mode switch" section, the owner), `/charly-internals:disposable`, and
`/charly-check:check` is rewritten to the source-confirmed model. Memory:
`gpu-driver-switch-wedge-rca.md`.

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî fix(preempt): correct concurrent shared-GPU arbitration ‚Äî serialized flip + process-liveness lease reconciliation (`v2026.167.1853`)

Two coupled fixes so multiple `requires_shared: [nvidia-gpu]` beds (e.g. comfyui +
jupyter-ml) BUILD and RUN concurrently while only the brief GPU driver flip is
gated ‚Äî never the pods themselves.

**1. Serialize the flip (the `driver=unbound` race).** A 16-way fan-out surfaced
`check-cachyos-comfyui-pod` failing instantly at acquisition:
`switch-to-nvidia FAILED: 0000:01:00.0 driver=unbound`. `ResourceArbiter`'s three
mutating methods (`AcquireShared` / `AcquireExclusive` / `ReleaseClaimant`) ran the
whole load-ledger ‚Üí decide ‚Üí GPU-driver-flip ‚Üí save-ledger sequence with NO lock,
so two claimants starting together both began the flip ‚Äî one unbound vfio-pci while
the other was mid-bind ‚Üí the device was left `driver=unbound`, the nvidia bind
failed, and both raced the lease-ledger write. Fix: the three methods now take a
blocking lock (the unified `acquireFileLock` primitive ‚Äî filelock.go) on
`~/.local/share/charly/preemption/.lock` around the whole acquire/release. The
first claimant flips the card and records its lease; the second blocks, then finds
the card already nvidia (idempotent ‚Äî no re-flip) and just refcounts. No
re-entrancy / self-deadlock: holder stop/start is in-process, nested `charly`
subprocesses are env-guarded (`CHARLY_PREEMPT_LEASE`) before any arbiter method, and
`reconcileStranded`/`removeLease` use `loadLedger`/`saveLedger` directly. Fifth site
on the one flock primitive (per-bed, deploy-config, build, harness/ledger, arbiter).

**2. Process-liveness lease reconciliation (the concurrent-shared CLOBBER the lock
EXPOSED).** Serializing the flip let a live concurrent R10 run far enough to surface
a pre-existing bug from the GPU-switch cutover: `reconcileStranded` (run at the top
of every acquire) judged a lease "stranded" via `a.running(lz.Claim)` ‚Äî "is the
claimant POD running?". But a TRANSIENT bed lease is created at the FIRST step of
the run, minutes BEFORE its pod is built/deployed; so the second concurrent
claimant's `reconcileStranded` saw the first, still-building bed's lease (pod not up)
and garbage-collected it as "claimant gone" ‚Äî two shared claimants clobbered each
other's leases (`leases=1`, never the refcount of 2). Fix: a lease's liveness is its
OWNER, not its pod. New `leaseLive` helper keys a TRANSIENT lease on its owning
process (the long-lived `charly check run` orchestrator) via PID + `/proc`
start-time (a PID-reuse guard so a crashed owner whose PID was recycled still reads
as gone ‚Äî crash-recovery must not hinge on luck), and a PERSISTENT lease on
`a.running(Claim) || ownerAlive` (the OR covers a `charly start` creator's own
bring-up window). `leaseLive` is used by BOTH `reconcileStranded` AND
`Status` (`charly preempt status`), so the display never disagrees with the GC
(R3/R5 ‚Äî one predicate, both surfaces). The lease records `OwnerPID`/`OwnerStart` at
creation (outermost process only ‚Äî nested subprocesses skip the arbiter). And
`reconcileStranded` now routes its teardown through the shared `releaseLeaseEffects`
(extracted from `ReleaseClaimant`, R3) so a genuinely crashed shared-GPU bed also
flips the card back instead of leaving it nvidia.

Follow-up (own cutover, R2 ‚Äî not this change): `AcquireExclusive` unconditionally
drops overlapping shared leases (exclusive-wins), which would yank a still-building
shared bed's lease ‚Äî by-design exclusive-wins semantics, tracked separately.

Regression coverage: `TestArbiter_TransientLeaseLiveOwnerNotReconciled` (a live-owner
transient lease whose pod is not running is NOT reconciled ‚Äî fails under the old
pod-running predicate), `TestArbiter_TransientLeaseDeadOwnerReconciled` (PID-reuse
guard via start-time mismatch), `TestArbiter_TwoConcurrentSharedLeasesCoexist`
(refcount=2, token nvidia).

R10 (`fully tested and validated`): `go test ./...` + `go vet` PASS (incl. 3 new
arbiter regressions); `task build:charly` fresh (`2026.167.1703`). Concurrent live
R10 of `check-cachyos-comfyui-pod` + `check-cachyos-jupyter-ml-pod` (both
`requires_shared: [nvidia-gpu]`, launched together from one `box/cachyos` project
dir): BOTH rc=0, all 10 steps `ok: true` incl. the `update` fresh-rebuild gate;
~6 min wall for BOTH (overlapped ‚Äî comfyui 168s, jupyter-ml 356s, wall ‚âà max not
sum, so the pods ran concurrently); a SINGLE gated `vfio‚Üínvidia` flip with the
nvidia-gpu refcount peaking at TWO coexisting active shared leases (the clobber is
gone); `driver=unbound` observations during the run: 0; post-run the card
auto-flipped back to `vfio-pci` with no leases left.

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî feat(build): version-keyed candy staging `.build/_candy/<candy>.<version>/` + `charly clean` retention (`v2026.167.1703`)

Replaces the single shared `.build/_layers/<candy>/` staging dir with a
VERSION-keyed `.build/_candy/<candy>.<version>/` (the candy's CalVer). Different
candy versions now occupy DISTINCT dirs, which fixes a crossover the atomic-swap
(`v2026.167.1601`) alone did not: two concurrent builds in one project dir that
resolve the SAME candy at DIFFERENT versions (e.g. divergent `@github` pins across
boxes) previously shared `_layers/<candy>/` and got last-writer-wins ‚Äî one build
silently COPYed the wrong version. Each version keyed to its own dir makes both
correct.

Cache-neutral by construction: a candy's CalVer changes iff the candy changes, so
the Containerfile COPY path (`.build/_candy/<name>.<version>/`) moves exactly when
its content does ‚Äî podman's content+instruction cache still hits on unchanged
candies. Containerfile generation verified byte-identical across repeat generates.

The BOX build dir stays un-versioned (`.build/{box}/`): a box's
`EffectiveVersion` is its highest candy version, so versioning the box dir would
change every box-level COPY path on ANY candy bump ‚Üí full box rebuild
(cache-hostile, against the build-speed goal). The box dir's own artifacts are
atomic single-version writes (no glob, no crossover), so versioning it buys
nothing correctness-wise. Crossover prevention lives where the bug class was: the
candy-derived, glob-installed staging.

`charly clean` now prunes outdated `.build/_candy/<candy>.<oldversion>/` dirs
(newest `keep_images` per candy ‚Äî the build-staging counterpart to image-tag
retention) AND removes the superseded `.build/_layers/` dir (unconditional, like
the makepkg sweep). The same prune auto-runs after `charly box build`
(`pruneBuildCandyDirs`).

R10 (`fully tested and validated`): `go test ./...` PASS incl. new
`TestPruneBuildCandyDirs` (keep-newest-N per candy + legacy `_layers` removal +
transient-temp skip) and the updated `TestCandyCopySource` (versioned path);
`task build:charly` fresh; generation verified deterministic; `charly clean`
live-verified (legacy `_layers` removed, current `_candy` kept); `check-pod` built
end-to-end from the versioned `_candy` dirs and PASSED (`ok:true`, `steps=10`,
0 `_candy` COPY errors, 79s).

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî fix(build): dev-localpkg staging clears stale CalVer ‚Äî regression from the atomic-`.build/` cutover (`v2026.167.1638`)

The atomic-`.build/` cutover (`v2026.167.1601`) dropped the per-image
`os.RemoveAll(imageDir)` at the top of `generateContainerfile` (it raced
concurrent shared-base builds), reasoning that stale leftovers are harmless
because the Containerfile COPYs by name. That holds for fragments/routes/inline ‚Äî
but NOT for the **dev-local-pkg charly toolchain**: `renderLocalPkgImageDevInstall`
stages the locally-built package into `.build/<image>/_localpkg/<candy>/` and the
Containerfile installs via a GLOB (`dnf install /tmp/charly-pkgs/*.rpm` /
`pacman -U ‚Ä¶/*.pkg.tar.zst`). Without the wipe, successive `task build:charly`
runs accumulated multiple CalVer builds of the package in that dir, so the glob
matched two versions ‚Üí `cannot install both opencharly-‚Ä¶1518 and ‚Ä¶1343:
conflicting requests` (fedora) / `duplicate target` (arch) on every charly-
toolchain image (`charly-fedora`, `githubrunner`, `charly-selftest`, `charly-arch`).
The 5-fedora R10 of `v2026.167.1601` missed it because those beds don't install
the charly PACKAGE via the glob; the 16-way fan-out surfaced it.

Fix: `renderLocalPkgImageDevInstall` now stages into a per-process temp dir and
installs it via `installDirAtomic` (the same `renameat2(RENAME_EXCHANGE)` swap as
`_layers`) ‚Äî the stage dir is REPLACED each generate, so only the CURRENT CalVer
is ever present, and the swap stays race-free under concurrent builds.

R10 (`fully tested and validated`): `go test ./...` + `go vet` PASS;
`task build:charly` fresh (`2026.167.1602`); `check-charly-fedora-pod` (the exact
bed that hit "conflicting requests") re-run all green ‚Äî `ok: true`, `PASS
(steps=10)`, the conflict gone, and exactly one package staged
(`opencharly-2026.167.1602-1.fc43.x86_64.rpm`); run concurrently with the 16-way
fan-out's tail (live parallel-safety demonstration).

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî fix(check): safe parallel `charly check` runs ‚Äî unified flock + race-free atomic `.build/` + DAG-aware build coordination (`v2026.167.1601`)

A hyper-parallel fan-out of all pod check beds (16 concurrent `charly check run`)
failed, and the RCA found TWO real shared-state races (NOT a "concurrency limit"):

1. **The `.build/_layers` race.** `.build/_layers` is a staging dir SHARED by
   every image in a project dir (not per-image). Concurrent `charly box build`
   processes in the same dir race: one's `cleanStaleBuildDirs` / `_layers`
   repopulation removes the dir mid-COPY of the other's `podman build` ‚Äî observed
   as `removing stale dir .build/_layers: directory not empty` and
   `COPY .build/_layers/rpmfusion/ /: no such file or directory` (`exit status
   125`). This is the same-project-dir `.build/` race the memory note flagged as
   "cross-image scope unverified" ‚Äî now confirmed: DISTINCT images in the same
   dir DO race on the shared `_layers`.
2. **The deploy-config lost-update race.** `saveDeployState` / `cleanDeployEntry`
   did an unprotected read-modify-write on the per-host deploy overlay
   (`~/.config/charly/charly.yml`); `charly config` / `charly start` took no lock
   at all (unlike `charly deploy add`, which already held the ledger lock). Two
   parallel beds could load‚Üímodify‚Üísave and silently drop each other's entry ‚Äî
   the truncation class the `loadDeployConfigForWrite` docstring warns about.

A separate trigger surfaced first and masked these: a YAML syntax error
introduced into `candy/container-nesting/charly.yml` (an unquoted `command:`
scalar containing `cut -d: -f1` ‚Äî the colon-space is the YAML "mapping values
not allowed" trigger) aborted every bed's candy scan in ~1s. Fixed by
single-quoting; that fix lands with the container-nesting cluster-B cutover.

**Fix, part 1 ‚Äî ONE unified flock primitive** (`charly/filelock.go`,
`acquireFileLock(path, blocking)`), replacing the two pre-existing ad-hoc flock
copies and serving every serialization site. `syscall.Flock` now lives in
exactly one file. The four call sites:

| Site | Lock file | Mode | Prevents |
|---|---|---|---|
| per-bed | `.check/<bed>/.lock` | fail-fast (`LOCK_NB`) | a 2nd `charly check run` of the SAME bed clobbering the 1st (its pre-run `charly remove --purge` / `charly vm destroy` would wipe the live target mid-test) |
| per-image build | `<dir>/.build/.locks/<image>.lock` | blocking | concurrent COLD rebuilds of the SAME image ‚Äî see part 3 |
| deploy-config | `~/.config/charly/charly.yml.lock` | blocking | the lost-update on the shared deploy overlay |
| harness | `.check/<score>/.lock` | fail-fast | (migrated ‚Äî `acquireHarnessLock` now delegates) |
| ledger | `~/.config/opencharly/installed/.lock` | blocking | (migrated ‚Äî `AcquireLedgerLock` now delegates) |

**Fix, part 2 ‚Äî race-free, deterministic `.build/` generation**
(`charly/build_stage_atomic.go` + `generate.go`). The shared `.build/` staging is
made concurrency-safe by ATOMIC writes, NOT by serializing the build (serializing
cold builds ‚Äî the long pole ‚Äî would be catastrophic for wall-clock). Every shared
write is atomic + idempotent + byte-deterministic, so a concurrent `podman build`
always reads a COMPLETE artifact and podman's content+instruction-keyed cache
still hits: the destructive `os.RemoveAll(_layers)`/`RemoveAll(imageDir)` are
gone; `_layers` is rebuilt in a temp dir and installed via
`renameat2(RENAME_EXCHANGE)`; the Containerfile, init fragments, traefik routes,
context-ignore, and content-addressed inline staging are written temp-then-rename;
`cleanStaleBuildDirs` skips the `_`/`.`-prefixed staging dirs (`_layers`,
`_buildconfig`, `.locks`). Containerfiles are confirmed byte-identical across
repeat generations (the cache-miss-avoidance the determinism guarantees).

**Fix, part 3 ‚Äî DAG-aware build coordination: serialize the shared intermediates,
parallelize the fan-out.** A PER-IMAGE build lock (keyed by image name under
`.build/.locks/`) is held across each image's build. When many beds in one project
dir start at once, the FIRST to reach a shared intermediate (a base like `fedora`,
or an auto-intermediate) cold-builds it ONCE while the others block on THAT image's
lock and then cache-HIT it ‚Äî so a shared base is built once, never N√ó redundant
cold builds ‚Äî while each distinct LEAF image takes its own lock so the leaves'
(cold) builds run FULLY PARALLEL. There is deliberately no per-dir build lock:
serializing the whole build phase would stall the parallel cold leaf builds.
Distinct project dirs (worktrees / box submodules) have distinct `.build/` trees ‚Üí
distinct locks ‚Üí unaffected.

R10 (`fully tested and validated`): `go test ./...` PASS (incl. new
`TestAtomicWriteFile_*` / `TestInstallDirAtomic_*` / `TestAcquireFileLock_*`);
`task build:charly` (binary fresh); Containerfile generation verified
deterministic (byte-identical across repeat generates). Per-bed lock ‚Äî two
concurrent `charly check run check-local`: one ran (`rc=0`), the other refused
instantly (`check bed "check-local" is already running in this project ‚Äî refusing
a concurrent run`). Config lock ‚Äî survived a 16-way concurrent run with `0` lost
entries. Parallel build ‚Äî the 5 fedora beds that previously died on the `_layers`
race (`check-pod`, `check-cross-pod-cdp`, `check-cross-local-http`,
`check-fedora-test-pod`, `check-jupyter-pod`) re-run concurrently from one project
dir (with the shared `charly` intermediate freshly cache-invalidated) all PASS
(`ok:true`, `steps=10` incl. the fresh-`charly update` step), per-image locks
(`fedora.lock`, `fedora-nonfree.lock`, ‚Ä¶ + `check-pod.lock`, `jupyter.lock`, ‚Ä¶)
confirmed present, `_layers` race signature eliminated; WALLCLOCK 380s.

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî fix(traefik): resolve `${HOME}` in the ACME storage path at build time (`v2026.167.1342`)

Found during the #23 traefik rootless-bind fix: `candy/traefik/traefik.yml` set the
letsencrypt `acme.storage: ${HOME}/.traefik/acme/acme.json`, but traefik does NOT
expand environment variables in its static config ‚Äî so it read the LITERAL
`${HOME}` path and SKIPPED the ACME resolver (`unable to get ACME account: open
${HOME}/.traefik/acme/acme.json: no such file`). A latent production bug (ACME
could never issue certs); no deterministic check exercised it, so it rode as its
own cutover after #23. Fix: a post-copy `run:` step resolves the placeholder at
build time ‚Äî `HOME_DIR=$(getent passwd 1000 | cut -d: -f6); sed -i
"s#\${HOME}#${HOME_DIR}#g" /etc/traefik/traefik.yml` (the `getent` pattern works
under both create and adopt user policies, like the sshd sudoers drop-in). A new
`traefik-acme-storage-resolved` `check:` pins it (asserts the on-disk config has
NO literal `${HOME}` and matches `storage: /home/`), so it fails without the fix.
R10: `check-fedora-test-pod` PASS (10 steps, all ok incl. check-live + fresh
update), 98s ‚Äî `traefik-acme-storage-resolved` PASSES alongside the #23
`traefik-websecure-port-open`.

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî fix(check): VM-target `charly check live` resolves cross-deployment peer vars (`v2026.167.1337`)

Surfaced by the #22 unified-readiness R10 (the `check-cross-vm-http` bed): a VM
SUBJECT bed whose check DRIVES a peer (a local host-driver curls the guest's
nginx via `${PEER_ENDPOINT}`'s ssh -L forward) failed with
`peer unreachable ‚Äî unresolved cross-deployment variable(s):
PEER_ENDPOINT:check-cross-vm-http:80`, then `check-live` retried to the 30m cap.
RCA ruled out, in order: a VMName-from-deploy-name bug (`checkVmTarget` correctly
returns the `vm:` field), a missing `-F` (both `SSHExecutor.sshBaseArgs` and
`sshForwardEndpoint` rely on the `~/.ssh/config` Include), stale-VM reuse (the bed
runner destroys the domain first), and the ssh-forward mechanism itself (an
isolated `sshForwardEndpoint` to a fresh `charly-web-vm:80` works). Root cause:
`CheckLiveCmd.runVm()` (the VM-target check-live path) was MISSING the
cross-deployment peer wiring its sibling paths already had ‚Äî the pod path
(`CheckLiveCmd.Run`) and the local path (`runLocalCheck`) both set
`runner.TargetResolver = liveTargetResolver(...)` (for the `on:` driver dispatch)
and call `applyPeerVarsSteps(...)` (to resolve `${PEER_HOST}`/`${PEER_ENDPOINT}`)
before `RunPlan`; `runVm` did neither, so a VM bed's peer-driven check could never
resolve its peer vars (no prior VM bed used them, so the gap was latent). Fix:
`runVm` now wires `TargetResolver` + `applyPeerVarsSteps` + `defer ClosePeers`
before `RunPlan` (R3 ‚Äî the same wiring the pod/local paths use). R10:
`check-cross-vm-http` PASS (6 steps, all ok incl. check-live + fresh update), 21s
(was 15min+ stuck retrying to the cap); the `local-driver-reaches-vm` check now
PASSES (`exit=0`, the guest marker fetched over the resolved forward). NOT a #22
regression ‚Äî #22's readiness primitive faithfully surfaced this pre-existing
check-live gap.

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî fix(openclaw): gateway binds loopback + runs unconfigured (rootless-startable) (`v2026.167.1314`)

Surfaced by the #22 unified-readiness R10 (the `check-openclaw-pod` bed): the
openclaw gateway supervised service was `running=false`. RCA in a disposable
container: the gateway exited at startup needing config (`Missing config. Run
'openclaw setup' or set gateway.mode=local (or pass --allow-unconfigured)`), and
with `--allow-unconfigured` it then hit a second guard ‚Äî `Refusing to bind
gateway to auto without auth` (in a container the gateway defaults to
`bind=auto`/0.0.0.0, which it won't expose unauthenticated). But the candy's
documented architecture is loopback-bind + socat relay (`port_relay: [18789]`),
and the exec was MISSING the matching `--bind loopback` flag (it relied on a
default that became `auto` in containers). Fix: the `openclaw` service exec adds
`--allow-unconfigured --bind loopback` ‚Äî loopback needs no auth, matches the
socat relay, and lets the headless gateway start before any operator setup. The
candy `description:` already claimed "loopback-bound gateway"; the exec now makes
that true. R10: `check-openclaw-pod` PASS (10 steps, all ok incl. check-live +
fresh update/feature-run-rebuild), 97s (RDD-verified the gateway reaches
`[gateway] ready` + serves HTTP). NOT a #22 regression.

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî fix(traefik): websecure entrypoint :443 ‚Üí :8443 (rootless-bindable) (`v2026.167.1231`)

Surfaced by the #22 unified-readiness R10 (the `check-fedora-test-pod` bed): the
traefik candy's `websecure` entrypoint bound the PRIVILEGED `:443`, which a
rootless uid-1000 pod cannot bind ‚Üí `listen tcp :443: bind: permission denied` ‚Üí
supervisord FATAL ("Exited too quickly"), so `traefik-service-running` was
`false` and the API probe got `connection reset by peer`. The candy already used
the non-privileged `:8000` for the `web` entrypoint ‚Äî the `:443` websecure was an
inconsistent oversight. Fix: `websecure.address: ":443"` ‚Üí `":8443"` in
`candy/traefik/traefik.yml` + the candy `port:` list + the description; this makes
traefik bind cleanly in EVERY rootless pod that composes it (box/fedora,
box/cachyos, root), and the web‚Üíwebsecure HTTPS redirect still works (now to
:8443). A new `traefik-websecure-port-open` `check:` (`addr 127.0.0.1:${HOST_PORT:8443}`
reachable) pins the entrypoint binds ‚Äî it fails without the fix. R10:
`check-fedora-test-pod` PASS (10 steps, all ok incl. check-live + the fresh
`update`/feature-run-rebuild), 111s (was 1889s ‚Äî the old run burned the full 30m
readiness cap on the crash-loop). NOT a #22 issue: #22's readiness primitive
faithfully surfaced this pre-existing candy bug. (The separate non-fatal
`${HOME}`-literal in the ACME storage path ‚Äî traefik does not expand env in
static config ‚Äî is a distinct latent bug, no deterministic check exercises it,
tracked separately.)

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî feat(check): unified load-robust readiness polling ‚Äî `pollUntil` replaces every fixed-timeout deadline (`v2026.167.1213`)

RCA of a heavy-parallel test fan-out (6 project dirs concurrent ‚Üí ~10 beds
failed at `check_s ‚âà 363‚Äì396s`): the failures were NOT bed bugs but charly's
own readiness waits hard-coded to a fixed `bedCheckReadyDeadline = 6m` magic
deadline (and a scatter of sibling fixed timeouts / `time.Sleep` poll-loops).
Under real CPU/IO contention a slow-but-PROGRESSING deploy blew the fixed 6m
and was killed prematurely ‚Äî so charly could not be driven in parallel. R4
forbids exactly this (a magic value must be NAMED, CONFIG-SOURCED, and
VALIDATED on load; a race is fixed with a synchronization primitive, never a
delay). This cutover removes every such literal.

ONE unified readiness primitive (`charly/poll.go`): `pollUntil(ctx, cfg, cond)`
where `cond` returns `(ready, progress, err)`. `progress` is a MONOTONIC
high-water marker; the no-progress watchdog aborts only after `NoProgress`
elapses with NO new maximum (a stuck deploy dies fast; a slow-but-advancing one
runs on), an `AbsoluteCap` is the hard never-hang ceiling, and a per-attempt
`context.WithTimeout` bounds any single probe so one hung call can never wedge
the loop. An `err` wrapping `ErrPollFatal` aborts immediately (auth/forward
death). Four builders express the call-site intents: `Wait` (monotonic,
no-progress + cap), `WaitCapped` (cap-only ‚Äî for a binary ready/not-ready
condition whose progress signal is too coarse), `WatchProgress` (no-cap
monotonic), `StopGate` (cap-only at the stop grace). Three poll classes
(`PollLocal`/`PollRemote`/`PollHeavy`) select the tick interval.

Every bound is config-sourced + load-validated (`charly/readiness_config.go`):
the new `defaults.readiness:` block (`poll_interval_local|remote|heavy`,
`per_attempt`, `no_progress`, `absolute_cap`, `stop_grace`; all Go
`time.ParseDuration` strings) resolves env (`CHARLY_READINESS_*`) > config >
named fallback const, then validates the RESOLVED ordering (each interval ‚â§
no_progress ‚â§ absolute_cap; poll_interval_local ‚â§ stop_grace ‚â§ absolute_cap) ‚Äî
on the post-env values, so an env override cannot smuggle in a nonsensical
bound. Absent ‚Üí the named fallback consts (`readiness*Fallback` in poll.go), so
existing projects are unaffected. The block is modeled in the CUE schema
(`#Readiness` in `charly/schema/box.cue`, reusing the shared `#Duration`) per
the `#Box` completeness invariant ‚Äî additive + optional, so no migration step
and no schema-version bump.

Twelve readiness/wait/stop loops across the codebase were unified onto the
primitive ‚Äî the check-bed runner (`check_bed_run.go`: `stepReady`,
`waitForContainerReady`, `waitForVmSshReady`; the fixed `bedCheckReadyDeadline`
/`bedCheckReadyInterval` consts deleted), VM deploy (`deploy_executor_ssh.go`
`WaitForSSH`/`WaitForCloudInit`; `deploy_target_vm.go` reboot boot_id wait),
the exclusive-resource arbiter (`preempt.go` `waitStopped` ‚Üí `StopGate`;
`holderStopTimeout`/`holderStopPoll` deleted), libvirt lifecycle (`libvirt.go`
shutoff-before-redefine; `vm_libvirt.go` `gracefulStopDomain`; the
`gracefulStopTimeout` const deleted), the guest agent (`libvirt_guest_agent.go`
`ExecAndWait`), SPICE (`spice_session.go` `WaitForDisplay`/`WaitForInputs`),
artifact collection (`layer_artifacts.go` `waitForArtifactPath`, FATAL on a
non-missing-file error), the cross-deployment ssh-forward
(`check_venue.go` `sshForwardEndpoint`), and the VM check-readiness gate
(`check_cmd.go`). Two loops were deliberately RETAINED (documented): the
`ProgressWatchdog` reference monitor (a distinct construct) and the
author-spec `runWithEventually` retry (its budget is the step's own
`eventually:`/`retry_interval:`, not a charly default).

Coverage: `charly/poll_test.go` (12 tests, fake-clock: advancing / frozen /
oscillating-crashloop / cap-only / binary-flip / fatal / transient /
per-attempt-blocking / ctx-cancel / ready / validation / builders),
`charly/readiness_config_test.go` (4: defaults, parse error, ordering rejected,
valid override), and `charly/cue_box_readiness_test.go` (the `#Readiness`
schema accepts a valid block, rejects a typo'd sub-key + a non-duration value +
a non-struct ‚Äî teeth-verified by removing the field and watching the ACCEPT
case fail). R10: a 4-lane concurrent bed fan-out partitioned by project dir
(recreating the contention that broke the old deadline) ‚Äî `check-k3s-vm`
(steps=6) + `check-arch-vm` (steps=13: SPICE, guest-agent, 8 libvirt-RPC
probes, VmDeployTarget add_candy, two nested-local beds) + `check-local`
(steps=4) all PASS on the fresh build with TWO VMs + heavy pod builds
co-resident; the readiness primitive deployed every bed, waited, and surfaced
real verdicts with no hang and no false-pass.

### 2026-06-16 ‚Äî feat(gpu): vfio‚Üînvidia driver-mode switch + refcounted shared GPU claims (`v2026.167.0747`)

`requires_shared:` joins `requires_exclusive:` / `preemptible:` on the
resource-arbitration axis (`DeploymentNode`): a SHARED claim ‚Äî refcounted, so
MANY claimants of one token run CONCURRENTLY ‚Äî on a host-resource token. For a
GPU-backed token the arbiter (`charly/preempt.go`) now flips the card's driver
MODE between `vfio` (VM passthrough) and `nvidia` (host CDI, shared across
rootless pods via `--device nvidia.com/gpu=all`); the driver mode is the real
mutual exclusion. The first shared claim flips the display function (`01:00.0`
only ‚Äî the audio function stays vfio-pci so the vfio-pci module never
deregisters), via `sudo` + sysfs `driver_override` (the chosen primitive:
`driverctl` is absent on hosts here and documented to hang on a running nvidia
driver; rootless `qemu:///session` `virsh nodedev-reattach` is Permission-denied
writing `driver_override`), generates the CDI spec AS ROOT
(`nvidia-ctk cdi generate --output=/etc/cdi/nvidia.yaml` ‚Äî `/etc/cdi` is
root-owned, so the user-level `EnsureCDI` cannot write it; `ensureCDIRoot`
reuses the sudo seam), and preempts any running `preemptible` vfio holder;
subsequent shared claims refcount with no further flip. An EXCLUSIVE claim
preempts ALL shared pods (stops them, does not auto-restart ‚Äî the operator
re-runs `charly start`, which re-acquires shared and re-flips to nvidia) and
flips to vfio; the last shared release flips back to the vfio default + restores
the preempted holder. New `charly vm gpu mode <vfio|nvidia>` operator verb (the
charly-CLI way to switch, vs ad-hoc sysfs). New `charly/gpu_driver_switch.go`;
`preempt.go` extended with shared leases + a `Mode` field + injectable
`switchMode`/`ensureCDI`/`resources` seams; `deployNodeSharesGPU` forces the CDI
device into a shared pod's quadlet even while the card is still vfio at config
time; `releaseExclusiveForClaimant` renamed `releaseResourceClaim`
(kind-agnostic). RDD-proven live on an RTX 4080 SUPER (the exact vfio‚Üínvidia‚Üívfio
sysfs recipe); R10: two ollama pods shared the card CONCURRENTLY (both saw the
GPU via CDI inside the container) and an exclusive claim preempted both + flipped
to vfio, then released cleanly back to the vfio default. The GPU POD beds
(comfyui / unsloth / immich-ml / jupyter-ml) gain `requires_shared: [nvidia-gpu]`
in the bed-rationalization cutover, which then measures them; the skill-doc
enhancement (`requires_shared` in /charly-internals:disposable,
/charly-core:deploy, /charly-vm:vm) rides with the plugins land.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(pixi): pin pixi candy to v0.70.2 + pre-commit `[project]`‚Üí`[workspace]` (`v2026.166.1751`)

The `pixi` candy now installs a PINNED pixi release: `var: PIXI_VERSION: v0.70.2` drives a
`releases/download/${PIXI_VERSION}/pixi-${BUILD_ARCH}-unknown-linux-musl.tar.gz` URL, replacing the
unpinned `releases/latest` form ‚Äî which made the SAME candy version install a different pixi over
time (non-reproducible, against the content-hash/CalVer build model). v0.70.2 was already the latest
release; the version `check:` now asserts the pinned `0.70.2`. The `pre-commit` candy's `pixi.toml`
moved off the deprecated pixi `[project]` table to `[workspace]` (pixi ‚â• 0.70 warns on `[project]`).
R10 (`analysed on a live system`): the pinned download fetched + extracted to `pixi 0.70.2`, and
`pixi install --frozen` on the `[workspace]` manifest succeeded with the EXISTING `pixi.lock` (no
regen ‚Äî the lock binds to resolved content, not the manifest table name) and zero `[project]`
deprecation. Commit `29f8c2e7`; plugins `9553c954`. (Surfaced by the `check-arch-vm` R10 of the
text-egress cutover, then taken on as its own cutover per R2.)

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(egress): CUE-validate rendered libvirt domain XML via koala (`v2026.166.1734`)

Sixth and final cutover of the CUE-egress-validation sweep. `RenderDomainXML` now runs
`ValidateXMLEgress` on its output: the rendered libvirt domain XML is decoded via CUE's EXPERIMENTAL
`cuelang.org/go/encoding/xml/koala` encoding (elements‚Üístructs, attributes‚Üí`$`-fields, text‚Üí`$$`)
and validated against the koala-shaped `#LibvirtDomainXML` envelope (non-empty `$type`/`name.$$`/
`memory.$$`), catching a broken render or `XMLPassthrough` snippet before VM create. BEST-EFFORT: a
koala *decode* error returns nil and defers to libvirt's `DomainDefineXML` (the authoritative gate);
only a schema violation on a successfully-decoded domain hard-fails. `Concrete(true)` catches an empty
`<name>` (koala maps an empty element to an absent `$$`). The earlier "CUE has no XML encoding" belief
was a stale web-search claim ‚Äî RDD against the installed `cuelang.org/go` v0.16.1 found the shipped
`koala` decoder. R10: `check-arch-vm` PASS 13/13 incl. fresh-rebuild; the rendered arch domain passed
the gate on both `vm-create` and `update`. Commit `a5b2e829`; plugins `e9d4993c`.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(egress): CUE-validate rendered Containerfile + service units (`v2026.166.1720`)

Fifth egress cutover. `validateTextEgress` + the `#RenderedText` string schema (`schema/egress_text.cue`)
reject the Go `text/template` `<no value>` nil-field marker, gating the two TEMPLATE-rendered text
artifacts: the Containerfile (`writeContainerfile`, both base + extra-image writes) and systemd/
supervisord service units (`RenderService`). charly does not set the template `missingkey=error`
option, so a render failure leaves `<no value>` in the output; the gate turns that into a hard
build/deploy error. Hand-built text (quadlet/shell/ssh/qemu ‚Äî no template) has no `<no value>`
failure mode and is deliberately NOT gated. R10: `check-arch-vm` PASS 13/13 incl. fresh-rebuild; the
Containerfile render (nested charly build) and the tailscale `.service` render both passed. Commit
`ea028442`; plugins `00521880`.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(egress): CUE-validate generated traefik dynamic config (`v2026.166.1706`)

Fourth egress cutover. `generateTraefikRoutes` now runs `ValidateEgress` against `#TraefikRoutes`
(`schema/egress_traefik.cue`) before `.build/<box>/traefik-routes.yml` is written: the hand-built YAML
must carry a non-empty Host rule, service name, and backend url (null routers/services tolerated when
no route candies). A candy with an empty host/port now fails the build instead of emitting a broken
proxy config. This cutover also DOCUMENTED the deliberate decision NOT to egress-validate pure
`yaml.Marshal(struct)` writers ‚Äî runtime config (`SaveRuntimeConfig`) and the deploy-state overlay
(`SaveDeployConfig`, already CUE-validated on ingress) ‚Äî which cannot malform by construction, so a
schema there would be validation theater. R10 (`analysed on a live system`): live `charly box generate
fedora-test` ran the gate and accepted the real testapi routes; `kubectl`-style validity confirmed.
Commit `def2ca82`; plugins `a2bee339`.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(egress): CUE-validate install-ledger records before write (`v2026.166.1658`)
