Third egress cutover. All four install-ledger write paths ‚Äî `WriteDeployRecord` / `WriteCandyRecord`
(host, atomic) and `AddCandyDeploymentVia` / `WriteDeployRecordVia` (guest, executor heredoc) ‚Äî now
validate against `#DeployRecord` / `#CandyRecord` (`schema/egress_ledger.cue`) via `ValidateEgressValue`
before the JSON is written. A record missing its identity/time fields fails the deploy instead of
silently corrupting teardown (the ledger drives `ReverseOps`). RDD correction: `#DeployRecord` requires
`deploy_id`/`target`/`deployed_at` but `image` is OPTIONAL ‚Äî a candy-only deploy legitimately has no
image (`deploy_target_vm.go`'s `if deployRec.Image == ""` fallback), which a too-strict first schema
wrongly rejected (caught by an existing collector test). R10: `check-arch-vm` PASS 13/13 incl.
fresh-rebuild; the nested local deploys wrote ledger records through the gate (in-guest ledger probes
PASS). Commit `b756537f`; plugins `8594e7ef`.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(egress): CUE-validate generated Kubernetes manifests (`v2026.166.1641`)

Second egress cutover. `GenerateK8sKustomize` now routes every emitted manifest through `writeK8sYAML`
‚Üí `ValidateEgressValue`: workload/service/pvc/ingress against the `#K8sObject` envelope (non-empty
`apiVersion`/`kind` + named `metadata`) and the base+overlay `kustomization.yaml` against
`#Kustomization` (`schema/egress_k8s.cue`). These validate charly's OWN typed-Go output, so they check
STRUCTURE (the egress failure mode) rather than deep per-field k8s API types ‚Äî that depth is an
INGRESS concern for user-authored manifests. Adds `ValidateEgressValue` (Go-value validation, no
marshal roundtrip). H3 RDD proved a full k8s schema vendors + compiles in 4.6 ms, but the envelope is
the right altitude for machine-generated manifests (no ~54K-line vendored bloat). R10 (`analysed on a
live system`): live `charly deploy from-box --cluster vm-k3s-vm` generated the tree through the gate;
`kubectl kustomize` confirmed valid k8s. Commit `7f27dfd8`; plugins `ae6b8baa`.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(egress): the CUE egress-validation foundation + `cue` candy + cloud-init (`v2026.166.1618`)

First egress cutover ‚Äî the counterpart to charly's CUE INGRESS validation: ingress proves the input
config (`charly.yml`), egress proves the config files charly WRITES to a system, before the bytes hit
disk. New `charly/egress.go`: `ValidateEgress` (serialized YAML/JSON) + a vendored-schema registry
(`registerVendoredEgressKind`) that compiles `package`+`import` schemas as their OWN `cue.Value` ‚Äî
they cannot join the package-less concatenated `sharedCueSchema` (`cue_schema.go`). cloud-init's three
seed files are gated in `RenderCloudInit`: user-data against Canonical's cloud-config schema vendored
offline via `cue import jsonschema:` (the new `task cue:vendor` pipeline + the new `cue` CLI candy,
pinned to charly's embedded `cuelang.org/go` v0.16.1), meta-data/network-config against closed
hand-authored schemas. New skills `/charly-internals:egress` (subsystem owner) + `/charly-tools:cue`.
Vendoring is dev-time only ‚Äî schemas convert to plain `.cue` and embed; nothing is fetched at
runtime (hermetic single binary). RDD proved import‚Üíbare-context-compile‚Üívalidate‚Üígenerate end-to-end
offline. R10: `check-arch-vm` PASS 13/13 incl. fresh-rebuild; the gate validated cloud-init live on
both create and the fresh `update`. Commit `abdbaaa2`; plugins `5a06c368`.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(loader): CUE-source the embedded default config (`charly/charly.yml` ‚Üí `charly/charly.cue`)

The binary-embedded default config ‚Äî the build vocabulary (`resource`/`builder`/`distro`/`init`)
+ the sidecar-template library (`sidecar:`) that every build inherits ‚Äî is now authored in CUE
(`charly/charly.cue`) instead of YAML. CUE was already the loader's decode + validation engine
(fed from YAML via `cueyaml.Extract`); this adds a CUE *source* front-end and points the embed at
it. Scope is deliberately bounded to the embedded default ONLY: project on-disk config stays
`charly.yml`. The write verbs ‚Äî `charly box reconcile`, the `charly migrate` chain, the
scaffold / `box set` / `add-candy` verbs ‚Äî are all `yaml.v3`-Node-based for comment preservation
and cannot operate on a `.cue` file without a CUE-AST rewriter; the embedded default is the one
config that is read-only at runtime, so it carries zero write-surface entanglement and is the
clean, fully-decoupled consumer of CUE-source authoring.

**One document-interpretation path, two source front-ends (R3).** New `charly/cue_source.go`
`compileCUEToYAML` compiles a CUE document with the existing `cueSchemaCtx`, requires it concrete
(`cue.Concrete(true)` ‚Äî a config is data, not a schema; CUE definitions + hidden `_` helpers
resolve at compile time and never export), and re-encodes it to YAML bytes that flow through the
UNCHANGED `mergeUnifiedDocs` core. The embedded `.cue` is parsed EXACTLY like any `charly.yml`
after the front-end ‚Äî no parallel CUE routing/normalize/merge. `embed_defaults.go` switches
`//go:embed charly.yml` ‚Üí `charly.cue` and runs the compile before `mergeUnifiedDocs`.

**Idiomatic, not mechanical.** The 1,373-line vocabulary was rewritten with CUE hidden-field
helpers + references that DRY the genuinely-repeated data ‚Äî `_pacmanCacheMount` / `_pacmanCache`
(the locked pacman cache, 5√ó), `_aptCache` (2√ó), `_dnfCache` (2√ó), `_bootstrapBuilderBase`
(pacstrap + debootstrap), `_homeArtifact` (npm + pixi `copy_artifact`) ‚Äî 13 duplicated
occurrences collapsed to 5 named helpers that resolve at compile time and never export. Distinct
per-distro logic (install / bootloader templates, package lists) stays explicit.

**Closed the embedded-vocabulary schema-validation gap.** `charly box validate` already unified
each `distro`/`builder`/`init`/`resource`/`sidecar` entity against its closed `#Kind` ‚Äî but only
for on-disk PROJECT files; the binary's embedded vocabulary (the richest in the system) was
decoded but never schema-validated. The shared loop is now factored into
`validateVocabularyCollections` (`validate.go`), called for BOTH project files and the embedded
default. `TestEmbeddedDefaults_SchemaConformance` validates every embedded vocab entity against
`charly/schema` ‚Äî and it passed with ZERO changes to the schemas (the earlier CUE-tightening had
already given them parity; they were simply never wired to the embed). Boundary: `schema/*.cue`
is the validation CONTRACT (binary-internal, not overridable); `charly.cue` is default DATA (fully
project-`charly.yml`-overridable via the gap-filling `applyEmbeddedDefaults` merge, and a project
override is itself `#Kind`-validated ‚Äî `TestEmbeddedDefaults_AllVocabKindsOverridable`,
`TestProjectVocabOverride_IsSchemaValidated`).

**Proof.** `TestEmbeddedCUE_DataEquivalentToLegacyYAML` asserts the CUE source produces a
`UnifiedFile` byte-for-byte identical to the frozen pre-migration YAML
(`charly/testdata/embedded_legacy.yml`, the verbatim deleted `charly/charly.yml`). Live on the
freshly-rebuilt binary: `charly box validate` (exit 0), `charly box generate` for all five distro
families (arch/cachyos ‚Üí `/var/cache/pacman/pkg`, debian/ubuntu ‚Üí `/var/cache/apt`, fedora ‚Üí
`/var/cache/libdnf5` ‚Äî the DRY helpers render correctly into the Containerfiles), and the
`check-local` disposable bed (deploy ‚Üí check-live ‚Üí fresh-update ‚Üí cleanup, PASS). The heavy VM
beds were not run: the embedded data is byte-identical, so a VM build is downstream-unchanged and
cannot fail differently (EXERCISE). No project migration or schema-version bump ‚Äî projects are
unaffected; only the binary-internal embed format changed.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(schema)!: CUE owns VM/libvirt validation + the firmware default

The immediate-next cutover after the validator-deletion (`feat(validate)!`, below).
The schema-tightening cutover had already recorded that `ValidateVmSpec` /
`ValidateLibvirtDomain` were TEST-ONLY (the closed `#Vm` CUE path has been the SOLE
production validator for VM/libvirt/cloud_init since the loader switch); the
validator-deletion swept `validate.go` / `validate_check.go` but never reached
`libvirt_validate.go`. This cutover finishes that, closes the one parity gap, and
moves the firmware default into the schema.

**Part A ‚Äî the Go VM/libvirt validators are DELETED.** `charly/libvirt_validate.go`
is removed in its entirety (546 lines): `ValidateVmSpec` and its whole tree
(`validateVmSource*`, `validateVmSnapshots`, `validateVmFirmwareMachine`,
`validateVmSSH`, `validateVmNetwork`, `validateVmCloudInit`, `ValidateLibvirtDomain`,
`validateLibvirtCPU` / `validateLibvirtDevices` / `validateLibvirtFilesystem` /
`validateLibvirtHostdev`, `validateLibvirtChannelPath`) plus the dead CPU-vendor
helpers `detectHostCPUVendor` / `readCPUInfoVendor` (the latter a never-implemented
stub returning an error, so the host-vendor‚Üî`vmx`/`svm` coherence check was
doubly-dead). All had no production caller ‚Äî only tests. Their coverage is migrated
to the table-driven `charly/cue_tighten_test.go` reject/accept guard (hostdev
PCI-hex + `managed` enum, filesystem `driver`/`accessmode`/`source`/`target`,
`autostart ‚áí libvirt` backend, the `clone`/`imported` source cross-arms). The dead
tests are removed from `vfio_test.go` / `vm_ssh_port_test.go` / `vm_snapshot_test.go`;
`ValidateLibvirtSnippet` (in `libvirt.go`, live caller in `validate.go`) and the
shared `boolPtrTrue` / `hexUintPtr` helpers stay.

The one PARITY GAP is closed by tightening `#Vm`: `firmware: uefi-secure` now
requires `libvirt.features.smm: true`. The renderer does NOT auto-enable SMM
(`buildDomainOS` emits the secure-boot `<feature>` toggles + secure `<loader>` but
never `<smm>`; `buildDomainFeatures` emits `<smm state='on'/>` only from an explicit
`features.smm`), so the deleted Go check was the sole enforcer. The CUE rule uses
required-field markers (`libvirt!: features!: smm!: true`) so it REQUIRES an explicit
declaration ‚Äî a plain `smm: true` constraint would auto-fill and silently pass. The
stale `/charly-internals:libvirt-renderer` claim that `uefi-secure` "additionally
sets `Features.SMM = true`" is corrected in the same change.

Four checks have NO CUE home and are DROPPED with note (all production-dead since the
loader switch, so zero behavior change): snapshot duplicate-`name` dedup (cross-element
uniqueness ‚Äî surfaces at libvirt apply time), the CPU host-vendor coherence check
(also inert per above), `<channel>` `/home/<user>` path-portability (needs the
`{{.VmStateDir}}` Go template context CUE lacks; the renderer's `expandVmPathTemplate`
remains the create-time path), and `kind: vm`-inline `libvirt.snippets` XML
well-formedness (the live `validate.go` path validates candy/image snippets only).

**Part B ‚Äî CUE owns the firmware default (unify-after-merge).** New
`charly/cue_defaults.go` `applyCueDefaults(kind, *entity)` marshals a RESOLVED entity,
unifies it with `#<Kind>`, and decodes back, materializing the schema's
required-with-default fields. It runs at the VM-create resolve point
(`vm_create_spec.go`, after the per-host instance-override merge and after backend
resolution ‚Äî so materializing `spec.Backend` there is inert), NOT at load: the loader
decode stays deliberately non-unifying so config + overlay merge still see
unset-as-zero. Only REQUIRED-with-default fields materialize (an optional-with-default
field stays absent on unify); a set or inherited value is never clobbered. `#Vm`'s
`firmware: *"bios"` thus becomes the single source of truth and the Go `empty ‚Üí "bios"`
fallback in `buildDomainOS` is deleted (the firmware `switch` already treated `""` and
`"bios"` identically, so the change is render-identical).

**Scope investigated and rejected.** Moving the generators (`k8s_generate.go`,
`cloud_init_render.go`, the libvirt input via `Decode`) or the cloud-init / k8s
defaults to CUE was scoped and rejected: the generation logic and those defaults are
irreducibly imperative (libvirt auto-pairing of shared-memory/idmap/passt, the k8s
workload-kind heuristic, cloud-init's `composeUsers` adopt-merge). Of the misc
string-default Go fallbacks, only `firmware` was a clean entity-field default;
`network.mode` / `cpu.mode` (absent-block construction + sibling `Model`/`Check`
defaults), `sharing` (a function parameter), `transport` (also read from baked OCI
labels), and `deploy.target` (an error-check, not a default) are entangled with
defaulting CUE cannot own, and stay Go.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(validate)!: CUE owns declarative validation ‚Äî split the Go per-entity validators

The immediate-next cutover after the loader switch. CUE is now the SOLE authority
for declarative validation (shape, type, enum, regex, range, required-field,
closedness); the hand-written Go per-entity validators are reduced to the
cross-entity / semantic checks CUE cannot express.

Four pure-declarative validators are DELETED outright ‚Äî `validateEnvFiles`
(PATH-in-env ‚Üí `#Candy.env`), `validatePort` (candy port range ‚Üí `#Candy.port`),
`validateRoutes` (route host/port ‚Üí `#CandyRoute`), `validateVersionFields`
(CalVer ‚Üí `#CalVer`) ‚Äî along with their orphaned helpers (`isValidPort`,
`calverRe`). Sixteen MIXED validators are SPLIT: each declarative sub-check moves
to its CUE constraint while the semantic core stays in Go ‚Äî `validateVolume`
keeps only duplicate-name detection (name regex + presence ‚Üí `#CandyVolume`);
`validatePortRelay` keeps dedup + relay-in-ports + the socat gate (range ‚Üí
`#Candy.port_relay`); `validateEngineConfig` keeps cross-candy conflict detection
(enum ‚Üí `#Candy.engine`); the dependency validators (`validateEnvDeps` /
`validateSecretDeps` / `validateMCPProvides` / `validateMCPDeps`) keep their
cross-section collision rules (name/description/key/url/transport ‚Üí
`#CandyEnvDep` / `#CandySecretDep` / `#CandyMCPProvide` / `#CandyMCPDep`);
`validateCandyTasks` keeps one-verb / required-modifiers / `${VAR}`-scope (var-key
+ mode ‚Üí `#Candy.var` / `#Op.mode`); `validateOps` / `validateCheck` keep
`Kind()` / verb-context legality / do:act / runtime-var scope / required-modifiers
(port-range, timeout, context enum, uid/gid, matcher operators, live-verb method
allowlists ‚Üí `#Op` / `#MatchOpMap` / the per-verb `#*Method` enums). The orphaned
helpers from the splits (`volumeNameRe`, `apkSourceAllowlist`, `secretKeyPattern`,
`validEngines`, `isValidEnvVarName`, `validMatcherOps`/`validateMatchers`,
`taskModePattern`, `taskVarKeyPattern`) are deleted with them.
`validateLocalTemplates` and `validateBuildTunables` are KEPT WHOLE ‚Äî the former
because the disk-read CUE pass can miss imported-namespace `local` templates its
candy-ref guard reaches, the latter because the `defaults:` block is not validated
against `#Box`.

Box validation is RE-WIRED to the resolved in-memory `cfg.Box` (was a
`box/*/box/*` disk glob), so CUE coverage matches the Go box validators per repo:
`validateProjectCUESchemas` marshals each `BoxConfig` back to its authored `box:`
wire form (injecting the map-key name `BoxConfig` does not carry) and validates it
non-concretely against `#Box` ‚Äî closedness + value constraints without forcing the
base/from disjunction to resolve, so a scratch box stays valid ‚Äî skipping disabled
boxes and the retired-tombstone `port:` field. Four schema gaps are tightened to
Go-validator parity: `#CandyVolume.name` regex, `#CandyAlias.command` required,
`#CandyExtract.{path,dest}` leading-`/`, `#Box.{jobs,podman_jobs_cap}` `>= 1`.

The deleted validators' unit tests are migrated to CUE reject/accept cases in
`cue_tighten_test.go` (the spec-is-the-schema regression guard); the now-redundant
Go tests are removed.

R10: `go test ./...` + `golangci-lint run` (0 issues) + `charly box validate` clean
on every box submodule (the tightened schema does not false-reject the real
corpus) + the representative `kind: check` beds (check-pod / check-k3s-vm /
check-local / check-charly-vm) through a fresh `charly update`.

### 2026-06-15 ‚Äî feat(loader)!: CUE-decode loader switch ‚Äî eliminate the custom YAML unmarshalers

The full loader switch (Cutover 1 of the CUE migration). The unified loader now
ingests YAML through CUE and decodes the data model via `cue.Value.Decode`
universally ‚Äî every entity, every load path (root-shape docs, candy manifests,
kind-keyed docs). The 15 custom data-model `UnmarshalYAML` shorthand decoders are
DELETED; their wire-shape canonicalization moves to a generic reflection-guided
normalizer (`charly/cue_normalize.go`, `NormalizeEntityNode`) that walks a YAML
node in parallel with the Go type graph and runs at load.

Mechanism (Option C): per-entity decode = clone YAML node ‚Üí normalize shorthand
to canonical struct form ‚Üí CUE ingest ‚Üí `Decode` (`charly/cue_loader.go`). Three
pillars: (1) json tags added across the data model (1032, matching the yaml tags)
so `cue.Value.Decode` maps snake_case keys; (2) the normalizer's per-type
expanders port each deleted unmarshaler's canonical mapping byte-for-byte ‚Äî
`PackageItem`, `PortSpec`, `ContainsList`, `ShellConfig`, `LibvirtGraphicsListeners`,
`PreemptibleConfig`, `TunnelYAML`, `DeployShellOverlay`; `EphemeralLifetime` gets
an `UnmarshalJSON` instead (its unexported `boolForm` defeats reflection); (3)
`Matcher`/`MatcherList`/`PortScope` keep `UnmarshalJSON` (the OCI-label JSON
transport) and lose only their dead `UnmarshalYAML`. Loader-envelope `ImportList`/
`ScanSpec` stay Go ‚Äî the import/discover graph resolution is unchanged.

CUE owns schema + validation universally (`validateProjectCUESchemas` /
`validateCandyCUESchemas` validate every kind against `#<Kind>` at
`charly box validate`). Decode parity was proven on the whole corpus (340
entities across all repos) before the switch. Because load-time normalize keeps
shorthand AUTHORING working, the originally-planned 639-file on-disk
normalization migration and the canonical-schema-tightening were unnecessary and
dropped (a net simplification; authors keep `port: 8080` shorthand). Load-time
candy typo-detection (unknown top-level key) is preserved by a Go guard
(`rejectUnknownCandyTopLevelKeys`); `keylint` suppresses the self-decoding
operator-map / shell types that no longer opt out of `KnownFields` via a custom
`UnmarshalYAML`.

R10: `go test ./...` + `task build:charly` + four disposable **fresh-rebuild**
beds ‚Äî `check-pod` (pod), `check-fedora-vm` (vm), `check-k3s-vm` (k8s-on-vm),
`check-arch-vm` (vm + nested host deploys) ‚Äî all PASS with zero charly-emitted
warnings; `charly box validate` clean on every box submodule. The redundant Go
per-entity validators (now duplicated by the universal CUE validation) are
removed in the immediate-next cutover (R2-separable: this cutover's R10 passes
without it).

### 2026-06-14 ‚Äî feat(schema)!: tighten all CUE schemas to closed Go-struct parity

The follow-on to the additive CUE-validation layer (below): the deliberately
**loose** first-pass schemas (open `...` tails on every def, blanket `{...}`
passthroughs for whole subtrees) are tightened to **closed** Go-struct parity.
A CUE `#Def` is closed by default; "tighten" = drop the `...` so an unknown key
is rejected (catching typos `yaml.v3` silently ignores), and replace every
blanket `{...}` with a modeled closed def. Per kind:

- **vm**: the two blanket lines `libvirt?: {...}` / `cloud_init?: {...}` become
  `#LibvirtDomain` (57 sub-defs mirroring `libvirt_yaml.go` ‚Äî features/cpu/clock/
  memory/numa/cputune/devices(disk/interface/graphics/video/‚Ä¶)/seclabel/‚Ä¶) and
  `#VmCloudInit` (6 sub-defs). The genuine typed-open hatches stay open and named:
  `xml_passthrough` (string), `snippets` ([]string), cloud_init `extra` (string),
  `network.ethernets` (`{[string]:{[string]:_}}`). Every `map[string]string`
  libvirt attr is a TYPED `{[string]: string}`, never a blanket. NB: `ValidateVmSpec`/
  `ValidateLibvirtDomain` are TEST-ONLY (never wired into production), so the CUE
  `#Vm` path is now the SOLE production validator for VM/libvirt/cloud_init ‚Äî
  these blankets had meant ZERO real validation of those subtrees.
- **deploy**: `sidecar`/`shell`/`probes`/`vm_state`/`#PortScope` blankets ‚Üí
  `#Sidecar`/`#DeployShellOverlay`/`#DeployProbes`/`#VmDeployState` (open tail ‚Äî
  machine-written runtime state) / typed `"all" | [...int] | {[‚Ä¶]: string}`.
- **k8s**: closed; `pod_default.tolerations` stays open (raw K8s Toleration objects).
- **box/candy/distro/builder/init/group/pod/sidecar/android/local/agent/module/
  target/resource**: closed; full field models from each Go struct.

Cross-cutting work: shared defs consolidated to ONE home in `_common.cue` (R3 ‚Äî
`#Security`/`#Size`/`#Shell`/`#ShellSpec`/`#PackageItem`/`#DistroPackages`/`#AUR`/
`#RepoBlock`/`#Duration`/`#CalVer`/`#EntityRef`/`#CandyRef`/`#PortPin`/`#VmSize`/
`#EnvVar`/`#InstallOpts`), deleting box's duplicate `#BoxSecurity`/`#BoxShell`.
A closed `#Op` (every authored yaml key of `checkspec.go`'s Op) + tightened
`#Step` (the 5-keyword disjunction embedding `#Op`) replace the open Op tail; the
live-verb method enums (`#CdpMethod`/`#WlMethod`/‚Ä¶) mirror the Go `*Methods`
allowlists exactly. **CUE closedness sharp edge:** an embedded `matchN(...)`
silently DISABLES struct closedness ‚Äî the three mutual-exclusion sites
(box base/from, candy apk package/apk, vm-ssh port/port_auto) use the
`{closed} & (arm | arm)` disjunction idiom instead, which preserves closedness.
**Scalar-coercion parity:** `yaml.v3` coerces an unquoted `PORT: 8080` into a
`map[string]string` string, so env-idiomatic value positions use
`#StrMap`/`#StrVal` (`string | number | bool`) to match Go and avoid
false-rejecting valid configs.

The tightening **surfaced eight latent bugs the loose schema had masked**, all
fixed in this cutover: a phantom Go `cdpMethods["check"]` keyed to a non-existent
`charly check cdp check` subcommand (the real one is `eval`, per the CLI + skill
+ corpus) ‚Üí renamed to `eval` and R5-swept across the map, the two
`validateCharlyVerb` tests, and a bench-bed prompt; `exit_code:` on four check
steps (the Op field is `exit_status` ‚Äî `exit_code` was silently dropped, so those
checks asserted nothing) in jupyter/jupyter-ml; `exclude_distros:` (plural; the
yaml tag is singular `exclude_distro`, so the exclusion never applied) in sag;
`autostart:` (the field is `auto_start`) in check-stack-layer; and **`device:`
(the `SecurityConfig` field is `devices`) in container-nesting + k3s-server ‚Äî
meaning `/dev/fuse` and `/dev/net/tun` were silently NOT being added to those
containers.**

Proven: `go test ./...` green (corpus 186/186 candies + 79/79 boxes + every kind
+ 29 reject/teeth tests that fail under the old loose schema); a live
`charly box validate` (exit 0) on the real project; and a fresh `check-k3s-vm`
image BUILD (the tight schema + the local fixed `k3s-server` candy built a real
VM image end to end). Because the tight schema validates candies WHEREVER
resolved, it correctly rejects the SAME latent bugs in candies fetched from a
pinned remote tag ‚Äî so landing is a B6/B7 cross-repo cascade: the superproject
publishes the fixed candies (new tag), each `box/<distro>` submodule
`charly box reconcile`s its `@github` candy pins to it (its build is then the
real consumer gate), and the superproject bumps the gitlinks. Making CUE the
SOLE authority ‚Äî deleting the now-duplicate declarative Go per-entity validators
(keeping the cross-entity graph/scope checks) + the explicit-`kind:`
normalization migration ‚Äî is the next CUE-authoritative cutover.

### 2026-06-14 ‚Äî feat(schema): CUE schema validation for all config kinds (additive)

The first phase of the CUE migration: a CUE-based validation layer over the
existing YAML config, with the **wire format unchanged** (YAML stays on disk;
CUE validates it). Each of the 18 config kinds ‚Äî candy, box, pod, vm, k8s,
local, android, deploy, check, agent, distro, builder, init, group, target,
module, resource, sidecar ‚Äî gains a hand-authored CUE schema in
`charly/schema/<kind>.cue`, embedded into the binary and compiled into ONE
shared instance (shared `#Step` / `#CacheMount` / `#PhaseSet` / `#Security` defs
live once in `_common.cue`, R3). A registry (`charly/cue_schema.go` + a per-kind
`charly/cue_kind_<name>.go` `init()` registration) maps each kind to its
`#<Kind>` definition; `Validate()` ingests each on-disk entity via
`cuelang.org/go/encoding/yaml` (`Extract` ‚Üí `BuildFile` ‚Üí `Unify` ‚Üí
`Validate(Concrete(true))`) and unifies it against that schema.

This step is **purely additive**: it runs alongside the existing hand-written Go
validators and removes none of them, so it is not a hard cutover. Proven against
the full real corpus (~343 entities across the superproject + all five `box/`
submodules) with rejection tests, the full `go test` suite, a live
`charly box validate` (exit 0) on the real project, and the `check-pod` R10 bed
(PASS, 10 steps). Making CUE authoritative ‚Äî tightening the schemas to parity
and deleting the declarative Go validators + shape-routing + the `yaml.v3` Node
authoring ‚Äî plus the explicit-`kind:` normalization migration is the follow-on
CUE-authoritative cutover, tracked separately. NB: `cue_kind_<name>.go` files
must not end in a `GOOS` suffix (e.g. `_android.go` would scope the file to
`GOOS=android`); the android registration lives in `cue_kind_android_reg.go`.

### 2026-06-14 ‚Äî feat(schema)!: one embedded `charly.yml`, parsed by the same loader (sidecar-root)

`charly.yml` was already the one-and-only config filename project-wide ‚Äî except
inside the `charly/` Go source, where the binary still carried **two**
differently-named embedded defaults, each parsed by its **own** code path:
`charly/build.yml` (the default build vocabulary) via a bespoke
`LoadEmbeddedBuildConfig` (`yaml.Unmarshal` into `UnifiedFile`), and
`charly/sidecar.yml` (the default sidecar-template library) via a wholly separate
`SidecarConfig` struct + `LoadEmbeddedSidecarConfig`, bypassing the unified loader
entirely (`sidecar:` was not even a recognized key).

This cutover consolidates both into a single embedded `charly/charly.yml`
(`git mv build.yml charly.yml` + the `sidecar:` section appended; `sidecar.yml`
deleted) and routes it through the **same** document-routing core as every other
`charly.yml`. The loop body of `loadUnifiedInto` was extracted into a shared
`mergeUnifiedDocs(merged, data, srcLabel, srcDir)` (classifyDoc ‚Üí
mergeUnified/mergeKindDoc); the new `embeddedDefaults()` calls it on the embedded
bytes, so the binary's own config is parsed EXACTLY like a project's. The two
bespoke embedded loaders + `embeddedBuildYAML`/`embeddedSidecarYAML` +
`applyEmbeddedBuildDefaults` are deleted; `applyEmbeddedDefaults` now also seeds
sidecar templates via the new `mergeSidecarMap`.

`Sidecar` becomes a first-class `UnifiedFile` field (+ `rootShapeKeys` +
`Config.Sidecar` + `DeployConfig.Sidecar`): a project may now declare a root
`sidecar:` template library that extends/overrides the embedded set, and deploy
resolution (`ResolveSidecarsForConfig(projectTemplates, deploySidecars)`) cascades
embedded ‚Üí project-root ‚Üí per-deploy. `SidecarConfig` survives only as the
`PodSpec.Sidecar` inline-list type.

Because `sidecar:` is now a recognized root key, this is an additive schema
change: a no-op `sidecar-root` `MigrationStep` (modeled on `peer-field`) raises
`LatestSchemaVersion()` to `2026.165.1048` so an older `charly` REJECTS a
root-`sidecar:` config (with a `Run: charly migrate` hint) instead of silently
dropping it; `calver-schema` re-stamps every versioned file. The
single-filename migration's redundant-`build.yml`-drop heuristic switched from a
raw `bytes.Equal` against the embed to a SEMANTIC compare of the parsed
distro/builder/init/resource maps (`localBuildMatchesEmbeddedVocab`) ‚Äî the
embedded bytes now also carry a `sidecar:` section a build-vocab-only `build.yml`
never has. `build.yml` remains a valid project-level flat-import filename; only
the embedded source file moved.

### 2026-06-13 ‚Äî feat(schema)!: collapse the five test/eval formats into ONE flat `plan:` vocabulary (plan-unify)

The capstone of the op-unify lineage. OpenCharly carried **five parallel
operation/test formats** layered on the `Op`/`Scenario` structs ‚Äî the imperative
install list `task:`; the baked acceptance `description.scenario:` with the
Gherkin step keywords `given`/`when`/`then`/`and`/`but`, the `Op.Do` axis
(`act`/`assert`/`instruct`), and the `setup:`/`step:`/`teardown:`/`on_fail:`
phase lists; `kind: recipe` (the scenario assembler with `from:` +
`select:`/`exclude:`/`prefix:`); `kind: score` (the AI-iteration benchmark
config); and `example:` (Gherkin scenario-outline row expansion). This cutover
**collapses all five into one vocabulary ‚Äî `plan:`, a flat ordered list of
intent-typed steps** ‚Äî and deletes every parallel code path. A candy is now
**declarative metadata (distro/package surface, `service:`, `port:`, `env:`,
`volume:`, `secrets:`, status) + ONE `plan:`**, nothing more.

A `plan:` step is exactly ONE intent keyword carrying prose plus an inline `Op`
(verb + matchers + `context:` + `id:`): **`run:`** (deterministic state-change ‚Äî
the install timeline, replacing `task:` and the build/deploy `do: act` steps;
lowered to the Containerfile / DeployExecutor, ledgered, and reversed by
`charly deploy del` exactly as `task:` was), **`check:`** (deterministic
idempotent probe, replacing `do: assert`; `charly check`/`charly check live` run
ONLY `check:` + `agent-check:` steps), **`agent-run:`** (an agent that may
mutate), **`agent-check:`** (read-only agent assessment, replacing the prose-only
`do: instruct` / `agent:` verb), and **`include: <kind>:<name>`** (splice another
entity's plan, replacing the recipe `from:` block). DELETED: `task:`,
`scenario:`, the `do:` axis, `given`/`when`/`then`/`and`/`but`, the
`setup:`/`step:`/`teardown:`/`on_fail:` phase lists, `kind: recipe`, `kind: score`,
`example:`, the `agent:` verb, and the `CtxAgent` context value (the `agent`
context folded into the `agent-*` keyword prefix). `context:` (`build`/`deploy`/
`runtime`) is kept; ordering uses step `id:` + `depends_on:[id]`; pod-targeting
and `count:`/`index_var:` are per-step (the latter replacing `example:` outlines).

The AI-iteration benchmark (was `kind: score` + `kind: recipe`) is now an
**`iterate:` block** on a `kind: check` bed (or a `deploy:`): `{agent, sandbox,
plateau_iteration, progressive, prompt, note, env, mcp_endpoint,
validate_ai_artifacts}`. The bed's own `plan:` IS the scored content;
`charly check run <entity>` drives the AI loop when the entity carries an
`iterate:` block, else runs the deterministic `kind: check` bed sequence. The
**scoring unit became the `check:`/`agent-check:` step** (was the scenario):
numerator = solved such steps, denominator = total such steps. Prompt renderers
`${SCENARIOS}`/`${RECIPES}` ‚Üí `${PLAN}` (the flat step list) and `${CHECKS}`
(the still-unsolved `check:`/`agent-check:` subset). Deleted: `HarnessScore`,
`HarnessRecipe`, `ResolveScore*`, `check_recipe.go` + `check_recipe_from.go`, the
`charly check recipe`/`list-recipe`/`list-score` commands; `ResolveScoreTarget` ‚Üí
`ResolveIterateSandbox`.

`description:` **collapsed to a plain string** ‚Äî the `Description{Feature,
Narrative, Tag}` struct became a scalar `description:` (the candy's purpose; first
line = the `charly box list` / `charly check list` summary). `feature:`/
`narrative:` nesting and per-feature `tag:` are deleted (tags are per-step now).
The download-verb extract filter modifier **`include:` was renamed to
`extract_include:`** (because `include:` is now the plan-composition step). The
ADE gate became "a non-empty `description:` string + a `plan:` with ‚â•1 `check:`
step" (`charly box validate` hard-errors otherwise). `charly candy add-scenario`
was removed (author plan steps by hand-edit or `charly candy set`);
`charly feature list/pending/validate` re-key to plan steps (`pending` lists the
`agent-run:`/`agent-check:` steps); `charly box/check feature run` run the baked
`plan:`, agent-grading the `agent-check:`/`agent-run:` steps.

OCI-label payload change: **`ai.opencharly.description`** (`LabelDescriptionSet`)
now carries `LabeledDescription{Origin, Description string, Plan []Step}` ‚Äî the
JSON key `scenario` ‚Üí `plan`, and `Description` is the string (was the struct).
The bake rule is unchanged in spirit (every `check:`/`agent-check:` step plus any
runtime-context `run:` step; pure build/deploy `run:` steps flow to the
Containerfile, not the label), re-keyed to `context:`; the legacy-accepting
`UnmarshalJSON` shim was deleted (hard cutover). Because every image carries this
label, the JSON-shape change required rebuilding EVERY image.
`ai.opencharly.check_level` is unchanged. Migration: the single idempotent
`charly migrate` gained a `plan-unify` step (schema CalVer `2026.164.0005`) that
prepends each entity's `task:` entries as `run:` steps, flattens `scenario:`
groups into the flat `plan:` (hoisting `setup:`‚Üí`run:` front, `teardown:`‚Üí`run:`
end, classifying each `step:` by keyword), collapses `description:` to the scalar,
and rewrites each `kind: score` into the target deploy's `iterate:` block with the
score's `recipe:` refs becoming `include:` steps. Docs swept across `CLAUDE.md`,
`README.md`, `VISION.md`, and the `plugins/**` skills + agents in the same cutover.

### 2026-06-13 ‚Äî refactor(check): dedup exact-content folded-eval twin scenarios

The op-unify cutover folded each candy's old `eval:` check list into `scenario:`
(preserving each check's `id:` as a single-step scenario named by that id),
ALONGSIDE the candy's authored ADE Gherkin scenarios ‚Äî which often already cover
the same check, producing redundant "twins". This removes the exact duplicates:
a folded-eval scenario (a single step carrying an `id:` and no Gherkin
`then:`/`and:`) is dropped when its step's check content is BYTE-IDENTICAL to
some ADE scenario step in the SAME candy ‚Äî provably coverage-neutral, since the
ADE step gives identical coverage. **715 twins removed across 182 main candies.**
Near-twins (same intent, different expression ‚Äî e.g. a live check using
`${HOST_PORT}` vs the ADE step's literal port) are conservatively KEPT (not
byte-identical ‚Üí not provably redundant). Reference-aware: scenario ids
referenced by a recipe `select:` (`sshd-binary`, `sshd-wrapper`,
`composition-source-charly`, `composition-source-marker`) are never removed. Box
submodules: 0 removed (their folded-eval scenarios are not byte-identical to an
ADE step). This is a one-off content cleanup, NOT a schema change ‚Äî there is no
migration step (a third-party config keeps its own scenarios) and `version:` is
unchanged. Verified: `charly box validate` exit 0 ZERO warnings across all 186
candies + `charly check run check-local` PASS + `charly check run check-k3s-vm`
PASS on the deduped candies.

### 2026-06-13 ‚Äî feat(schema)!: rename the evaluation harness verb `eval` ‚Üí `check` (full sweep)

The evaluation harness's verb renamed from `eval` to `check` everywhere, so the
CLI verb matches the `charly.yml` verb (the standing guidance) ‚Äî the deferred
sibling of the same-day Op-unification cutover below. This was a **full sweep**:
the CLI command `charly eval [box|live|run|cdp|wl|dbus|vnc|mcp|record|spice|
libvirt|k8s|adb|appium|feature]` ‚Üí `charly check ‚Ä¶`; the root `eval:` bed-registry
key ‚Üí `check:` and `kind: eval` ‚Üí `kind: check`; the per-box `eval_level:` field ‚Üí
`check_level:` (baked label `ai.opencharly.eval_level` ‚Üí `ai.opencharly.check_level`);
`defaults.keep_eval_runs` ‚Üí `keep_check_runs`; the run-artifact dir `.eval/` ‚Üí
`.check/`; the `eval-*` bed names (`eval-pod`‚Üí`check-pod`, `eval-local`‚Üí
`check-local`, `eval-k3s-vm`‚Üí`check-k3s-vm`, ‚Ä¶) and the `candy/eval-*-layer`
candy dirs ‚Üí `check-*`; the `/charly-eval:*` skill plugin ‚Üí `/charly-check:*`
(`plugins/eval/`‚Üí`plugins/check/`, the `eval` orchestrator skill ‚Üí`check`,
`eval-k8s`‚Üí`check-k8s`, `eval-sway-browser-vnc`‚Üí`check-sway-browser-vnc`, the
`eval-bed-runner` agent ‚Üí`check-bed-runner`, the `/triage-eval-failure` workflow
‚Üí`/triage-check-failure`). 63 Go `eval_*.go` files renamed to `check_*.go`;
`EvalCmd`‚Üí`CheckCmd` and the whole harness identifier set renamed.

**Deliberately preserved** (NOT the harness): the Chrome DevTools Protocol JS
`eval` method (`charly check cdp eval`, the `cdp: eval` YAML verb value,
`CdpEvalCmd`, `cdpEvaluate`, `Runtime.evaluate`); the Go stdlib
`filepath.EvalSymlinks`; the external Python packages `pure_eval` /
`eval-type-backport` in pixi locks; and `charly doctor`'s pre-existing
dependency-check types (renamed `CheckStatus`/`CheckResult` ‚Üí
`DoctorCheckStatus`/`DoctorCheckResult` so the harness owns the bare names).
`EvalCheckFailExitCode` de-doubled to `CheckFailExitCode`.

Migration: `migrate_eval_check.go` (schema `2026.164.0003`; HEAD bumped to
`2026.164.0004`) renames the schema TOKENS (`eval:`‚Üí`check:`, `eval_level:`‚Üí
`check_level:`, `keep_eval_runs:`‚Üí`keep_check_runs:`, `kind: eval`‚Üí`kind: check`)
but never author entity NAMES ‚Äî a third-party config keeps its own names. Box
submodule `@github` candy refs (`candy/eval-*-layer`) repoint to `candy/check-*`
at the producer's new tag (B6 cross-repo staged landing).

### 2026-06-13 ‚Äî feat(schema)!: unify task: + eval: + agent: into one generic `Op` vocabulary; fold eval: into scenario:

The candy/box config carried THREE parallel, duplicated operation vocabularies ‚Äî `task:` (imperative install/build verbs), `eval:` + `description.scenario` (declarative check verbs, written TWICE in most candies), and a proposed free-form agent surface ‚Äî backed by two Go structs (`Task` + `Check`), two verb lists (`TaskVerbs` + `CheckVerbs`), two `Kind()`/validator triples, and a doubled candy YAML. This single-phase hard cutover collapses all of it into ONE generic `Op` struct with three orthogonal axes ‚Äî **verb** (the union set) √ó **`do:`** (`act`|`assert`|`instruct`) √ó **`context:`** (`build`|`deploy`|`runtime`|`agent`) ‚Äî driven by ONE source of truth, the `VerbCatalog` map (`verb ‚Üí {Contexts, DefaultDo, Reversible, LowersTo}`).

**Go.** `Task` + `Check` ‚Üí one `Op` (`evalspec.go`) carrying every former field plus the `do:`/`context:` axes and the `agent:` verb; `TaskVerbs`/`CheckVerbs`/the two `Kind()` triples deleted in favor of `OpVerbs` + `VerbCatalog`. `Step` embeds `Op` inline; `Scenario` split out of `Description` to a top-level sibling on candy/box/pod/vm specs (`description:` keeps `{feature, narrative, tag}`). The InstallPlan IR renamed `TaskStep`‚Üí`OpStep` (`StepKindTask`‚Üí`StepKindOp`), `Task *Task`‚Üí`Op *Op`; `compileTaskSteps`‚Üí`compileOpSteps` gained act-mode lowering (a `do:act` `package`‚Üí`SystemPackagesStep`, `service`‚Üí`ServicePackagedStep` ‚Äî reusing the typed step's emit + `Reverse()`, never reinventing reversal) and folds build/deploy-scoped `do:act` ops from the scenario list into the install timeline; the OCI/local/VM emitters renamed `emitTask`‚Üí`emitOp`, `execTask`‚Üí`execOp`, `renderTaskCommand`‚Üí`renderOpCommand`. `runOne` (`evalrun.go`) gained the `do:` branch: `assert` = the existing probe handlers; `act` executes state-provision verbs via the executor (`evalrun_act.go`); `instruct` (and the `agent:` verb) routes to the agent grader. `file` is a probe (its act form is the `write`/`copy` verbs); `user`/`group`/`kernel-param`/`mount` act at runtime via the executor (build/deploy file creation is `write`/`copy`), and the validator rejects a `do:act` op with no build/deploy install path so the compiler never silently drops one.

**Deletions (R5).** The `ai.opencharly.eval` OCI label + `LabelEvalSet` + the candy/box `eval:`/`deploy_eval:` flat check fields + `evalcollect.go` (`CollectEval`/`MergeDeployEval`) + the `Check.Scope` field are gone; `MergeDeployDescriptions` ports the override-by-id rules. The candy YAML key allowlist dropped `tests:`/`eval:` and gained `scenario:`.

**Per-box `eval_level` ladder.** A new `BoxConfig.EvalLevel` (`none`|`build`|`noagent` (default)|`agent`, `eval_level.go`) gates how deep `charly eval run <bed>` drives a box's acceptance ‚Äî baked as the `ai.opencharly.eval_level` capability label and read by the bed runner (`runEvalBed`) to skip build-acceptance (`none`), runtime-acceptance (`build`), or to enable the prose-step agent grader (`agent`); `noagent` preserves the prior full sequence.

**Migration.** `charly migrate` gained the `op-unify` step (schema `2026.164.0001`, HEAD now `2026.164.0002`): per candy/box/pod/vm/deploy/recipe/score/eval-bed entity it hoists `description.scenario:`‚Üítop-level `scenario:`, folds every `eval:`/`deploy_eval:` SequenceNode check into `scenario:` preserving each check's `id:` as the scenario name (so recipe `select:`/`exclude:`/`depends_on:` references stay valid, including cross-repo into the box submodules ‚Äî de-duplicating a check that twins a description scenario is a deliberate reference-aware per-candy follow-up, NOT a reference-blind migration), rewrites `task:` `cmd:`‚Üí`command:` + run-as `user:`‚Üí`run_as:`, rewrites check `scope:`‚Üí`context:`, and strips the retired recipe-`from:` `scope:`/`skip_live_only:` filters. The ROOT harness `eval:` block (a MAPPING of bed name ‚Üí deploy node) is left untouched ‚Äî only a SequenceNode `eval:` (a check list) folds.

The `charly eval`‚Üí`charly check` command rename (deferred, separable: this cutover's claim ‚Äî one unified `Op` vocabulary, eval folded into scenario ‚Äî holds without it) lands as its own immediate-next cutover.

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî docs(policy): trim CLAUDE.md prose; restore the load-bearing attribution-tier rows

A working-tree edit trimmed `CLAUDE.md` toward "rules and mandates ONLY": it removed the R0 "Rationalizations that are NOT defences" subsection, the "Enforcing VISION.md" tenet-binding table (the 10-row tenet ‚Üí mandate ‚Üí skill map), the intro "Six parts" overview sentence, and the Key Rules "Documentation-only change class" bullet ‚Äî and reworded the intro to name QEMU/libvirt as deploy substrates. The R5 cross-reference validation cleared all four removals: nothing references them (the `root-cause-analyzer` "Forbidden Rationalizations" section is its own R1 flake-excuse list, not a reference to the removed R0 subsection; the "Documentation-only change class" stays defined in the R10 bullet + AI Attribution). But the same trim also deleted the `syntax check only` and `theoretical suggestion` rows from the AI-Attribution tier table ‚Äî and those are LOAD-BEARING: `pre-commit-gate.sh` names both (it blocks `syntax check only` with a custom message and rejects `theoretical suggestion` as forbidden-for-shipped-code), and four skill/agent surfaces mirror them (`testing-validator`, `/charly-eval:eval`, `/charly-internals:disposable`, `/charly-internals:agents`). The 5-row table over a 3-entry `LEGAL` commit set is intentional ‚Äî two tiers are documented-but-commit-forbidden, so the hook's block messages must reference defined tiers ‚Äî so both rows were restored verbatim. Two confusions the trim introduced were resolved: the R0 sentence regained its terminal period (`domain** R0 dictates` ‚Üí `domain.** R0 dictates`), and the intro VM-backend casing was normalized to repo canon (`Qemu or Libvirt` ‚Üí `QEMU, or libvirt`, Oxford comma per house style). Documentation-only change class ‚Äî `CLAUDE.md` prose only, zero behavior change; gated by the non-runtime standards (R5 grep self-test, cross-reference validation against the hook's `LEGAL` set and the four mirroring skills, markdown-table integrity) at the `documentation reviewed` tier.

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî fix(hooks): `documentation reviewed` accepts a submodule pointer bump to an all-documentation commit

The `documentation reviewed` tier (added earlier today) had a blind spot: a docs-only **skill** cutover edits a `*.md` under the `plugins` submodule, so its superproject half is a *gitlink-only* commit. `pre-commit-gate.sh`'s `assert_docs_only_diff` classified the staged path `plugins` as non-documentation (no extension ‚Üí neither a doc path nor a recognized comment-only code file), so it BLOCKED `documentation reviewed` on the exact commit a docs-only skill cutover requires ‚Äî and the runtime tiers are dishonest for prose, leaving no legal honest tier. The gap went unnoticed because the introducing commit (`67fde778`) also edited the hook, so its superproject commit legitimately took a runtime tier and the bump rode along; a pure gitlink-only docs commit was never exercised against the new gate.

The gate now DERIVES a pointer bump's doc-ness from what it points at. `assert_docs_only_diff` iterates `git diff --cached --raw` (which exposes the gitlink mode `160000` + the old/new SHAs) and, for a staged submodule change, RECURSES: it runs the same doc/comment-only predicate over the submodule's own `old..new` diff. A bump to an all-documentation submodule commit counts as documentation (`documentation reviewed` is legal); a bump that integrates submodule code is rejected (the commit takes a runtime tier); a bump it cannot certify ‚Äî submodule objects absent locally, or a submodule add/remove (all-zero old/new sha) ‚Äî is blocked conservative-safe. No new tier: the taxonomy stays at five, and doc-ness is self-correcting. A secondary correctness fix scopes the gate's index inspection to the repo a `git -C <dir> commit` actually targets (previously it always inspected the hook's CWD), so a docs+code commit made *inside* a submodule is judged against the submodule's own index.

Surfaces swept (claim-keyed, R5) so every enumeration of "all-documentation" now includes the certified pointer bump: `CLAUDE.md` (tier table, the boundary paragraph, the R10 "Documentation-only change class" bullet, the Key Rules anchor); `pre-commit-gate.sh` (logic + header comments); `/charly-eval:eval` (the "R10 gate by change class" row + the mixed-changes note); `/charly-internals:git-workflow` (B2 gained a pointer-bump attribution rule ‚Äî both halves of a docs-only skill cutover land at `documentation reviewed`); `/charly-internals:agents` (hooks doctrine); `testing-validator`; `strict-policy`; `cutover-policy`. Verified live (the hook/script change class = parse + execute the changed script): an isolated repo + submodule exercising 11 cases ‚Äî docs bump ‚Üí pass, code bump ‚Üí block, uncertifiable bump ‚Üí block, regular docs ‚Üí pass, regular/mixed code ‚Üí block, both `-C` scoping directions, illegal tier ‚Üí block, runtime-tier-with-code ‚Üí pass ‚Äî all green. MIXED change class (behavioral hook edit + docs): the `plugins` commit (all `*.md`) lands at `documentation reviewed`; the superproject commit (the hook + `CLAUDE.md` + this entry + the pointer bump) lands at `fully tested and validated`. This superproject pointer bump also finally carries the previously-pushed `git-workflow` "right worktree" invariant (`plugins` `69b74f0d`) ‚Äî pin ONE absolute worktree path for the whole edit‚Üícommit‚Üíland sequence; verify `git rev-parse --show-toplevel`, since under symlinked / near-twin sibling worktrees a `cd` to the wrong sibling makes `git switch -c` + `git commit` run against a clean tree and silently land nothing ‚Äî into the superproject.

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî feat(policy): a `documentation reviewed` attribution tier + accurate Claude-involved-vs-human attribution scope

Added a fifth AI-attribution tier, **`documentation reviewed`**, as the honest tier for the **Documentation-only change class** (`*.md` files or comment-only code edits, zero behavior change), and DELETED the prior kludge whereby docs-only cutovers borrowed the runtime tier `fully tested and validated` "per the provision". The four pre-existing tiers are all runtime-verification statements (full R10 + fresh rebuild; a live invocation ran; compile-only); documentation has no runtime to grade, so stamping a Markdown edit "fully tested and validated [on a live system]" was a false claim the attribution system exists to prevent. `documentation reviewed` is earned when ALL non-runtime standards pass (adversarial consistency review, R5 grep self-test, cross-reference validation, markdown integrity, the PreToolUse gates); it is FORBIDDEN the moment a cutover also touches code/config (that surface takes a runtime tier and the docs ride along). The class fixes the gate; the gate fixes the tier ‚Äî `analysed on a live system` and `syntax check only` remain partial-completion waypoints for the runtime classes only, and the Documentation-only class (no live runner) has no waypoint.

Made the attribution SCOPE accurate: "ALL commits MUST carry an `Assisted-by: Claude (<confidence>)` trailer" ‚Üí **every commit Claude is involved in ‚Äî in ANY way ‚Äî MUST attribute** (if Claude touched it at all the classification is correct; when unsure, attribute), while a purely human-authored hand-commit with ZERO Claude involvement carries none. No behavioral loosening: `pre-commit-gate.sh` is wired PreToolUse(Bash)-only, so a human's own terminal commit never passes through it ‚Äî the "accept human commits" requirement was already satisfied by the wiring, and this only makes the wording match. The gate continues to demand the trailer on every Claude-run commit.

`pre-commit-gate.sh` gained `documentation reviewed` in its legal-on-commit set AND a strict, conservative-safe coherence check: when the tier is `documentation reviewed`, it inspects `git diff --cached` and BLOCKS unless every staged file is a documentation path (`*.md`/CHANGELOG/README/LICENSE/VISION/`*.txt`) or a code file whose staged hunks are full-line comments/blanks only ‚Äî it may conservatively reject a trailing/block-comment edit (harmless) but never lets a behavioral change pass as docs (proven live across 15 branches in an isolated repo). Surfaces swept (claim-keyed, R5): `CLAUDE.md` (the tier table, the scope mandate, the R10 "Documentation-only change class" bullet, the Key Rules anchor, the deleted provision paragraph); the `pre-commit-gate.sh` hook; `/charly-eval:eval` (the "R10 gate by change class" matrix gained a "Tier on a clean pass" column + a waypoint note ‚Äî the canonical class ‚Üí gate ‚Üí tier cross-walk); `testing-validator` (tier table + provision); `/charly-internals:agents` (the hooks-doctrine gate description); `root-cause-analyzer` (Step 7); `git-workflow` (report format); `cutover-policy` ("when the policy might not apply"); `strict-policy` (R1 docs-divergence paragraph); and `/charly-internals:skills` (mirroring surfaces + the Authoritative-copy registry).

MIXED change class ‚Äî docs/policy-only (every `*.md`) PLUS a behavioral hook-script edit (`pre-commit-gate.sh`): no `MigrationStep`, no `version:` bump. The `plugins` submodule commit (all `*.md`) self-demonstrates the new tier ‚Äî it lands at `documentation reviewed`; the superproject commit (which edits the hook) lands at a runtime tier. The 5 `box/*/README.md` bare `*Assisted-by: Claude*` trailers (no tier) were deliberately left to a separate cutover.

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî docs(policy): documentation/skill/comment divergence is a first-class R1 incident

Sharpened R1/R2/R5 in `CLAUDE.md` (no new section, no R-number/heading rename) so that ANY divergence between a doc, skill, or code comment and observed reality ‚Äî discovered by ANY means, not only via an RDD bed-contradiction or an R5 deleted-identifier ‚Äî is an incident: it triggers `/charly-internals:root-cause-analyzer` (R1), its RCA remediation is a TRANSITIVE *claim-keyed* sweep across EVERY other doc/skill/comment carrying the same false/outdated/misleading claim (generalizing R5's identifier-keyed `git grep` self-test), and the fix for the changed surface + its sibling-set is BLOCKING in the current cutover (blocking by R2's own "is the tree correct?" test). A genuinely-unrelated divergence stumbled upon mid-cutover is still RCA'd immediately and never parked as "someday", but lands as its own immediate-next cutover (R2's existing non-blocking path). Previously this was covered only narrowly and implicitly ‚Äî RDD's "when the bed contradicts the doc, the DOC IS STALE" (bed-discovery only) and R5's stale-reference sweep (deleted-identifier only); both are now framed as special cases of the general rule.

Surfaces: `CLAUDE.md` R1/R2/R5 (the mandate); `/charly-internals:strict-policy` R1 (a new "Documentation divergence is a failure for R1 purposes" paragraph), R2 (a documentation worked-example of the existing blocking/non-blocking discriminator), R5 (identifier-keyed vs claim-keyed sweep) ‚Äî the operationalization; the `root-cause-analyzer` agent ("What Qualifies as Unexpected" + a Step 7 transitive-sweep duty + "When to Invoke"); and `/charly-internals:skills` "When to Update Skills" (one general divergence row, with the two prior RDD/R5 rows reframed as special cases). The Authoritative-copy registry is unchanged (R1‚ÄìR5 already ‚Üí strict-policy); no new owner, no new named section.

Docs/policy-only cutover (every touched file is `*.md`, zero behavioral change): no `MigrationStep`, no `version:` / `LatestSchemaVersion()` bump. Gate = the non-runtime standards (CLAUDE.md R10 "Docs / comments only"): adversarial consistency review (R1/R2/R5 in `CLAUDE.md` ‚Üî strict-policy ‚Üî the agent all say the same thing), R5 grep self-test, cross-reference validation, markdown integrity, the PreToolUse commit/push gates. Deliberately untouched (audited): no `CLAUDE.md` heading / R-number / clause rename ‚Üí the mirroring-surface sweep (hooks, other agents, signpost `CLAUDE.md` files, workflows) is NOT triggered; those reference R1/R5 by name as pointers and stay valid. Landed across plugins + the superproject.

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî feat(schema)!: `kind: ai` ‚Üí `kind: agent`, strict canonical fixed-width CalVer, and the human/AI voice collapsed to "you"

Three intertwined cutovers landed together (schema HEAD `2026.161.2303` ‚Üí `2026.163.0928`).

**`kind: ai` ‚Üí `kind: agent`.** The reusable agent-CLI catalog kind was renamed end-to-end: the catalog map key `ai:` and the `kind: score` eligible-agent selector `ai:` ‚Üí `agent:`, the standalone-doc discriminator `kind: ai` ‚Üí `kind: agent`, the Go surface (`AIConfig`‚Üí`AgentConfig` + file `ai_config.go`‚Üí`agent_config.go`, `AIDoc`‚Üí`AgentDoc`, `UnifiedFile.AI`‚Üí`.Agent`, `kindKeyedDoc.AI`‚Üí`.Agent`, `mergeAIMap`‚Üí`mergeAgentMap`, `ResolveAI`/`SortedAINames`/`PrintAIs`/`ErrNoAIs`/`ErrAINotFound`/`ParseAITimeout`/`DefaultAITimeout`/`AIOutputFormat*`/`RunAIOnce`/`AIName`‚Üí`AgentName`, `EvalListAICmd`‚Üí`EvalListAgentCmd`, `resolveGraderAI`‚Üí`resolveGraderAgent`, `AgentGrader.AI`‚Üí`.Agent`, `HarnessOpts.AI`/`HarnessScore.AI`/`FinalReport.AI`‚Üí`.Agent`), the CLI (`--ai`‚Üí`--agent` on every flag, `charly eval list-ai`‚Üí`list-agent`), the runtime env var `CHARLY_EVAL_AI`‚Üí`CHARLY_EVAL_AGENT`, and `ai_version:`‚Üí`agent_version:` in result files. A new idempotent `agent-kind-rename` `MigrationStep` (`migrate_agent_kind_rename.go`) rewrites `ai:`/`kind: ai` ‚Üí `agent:`/`kind: agent` in project + per-host configs; the loader's `rejectLegacyAgentCatalog` hard-rejects a residual `ai:` with a `charly migrate` hint, and `rootShapeKeys` gained `agent` (a kind that also has the inline catalog form must be in BOTH `kindKeys` and `rootShapeKeys`, else it reads as pure-kind-keyed and the doc is "ambiguous"). The independent `kind: score` `validate_ai_artifacts` flag is a DIFFERENT concept (validate the artifact the runner produced, not the catalog) and was deliberately NOT renamed.

**Strict canonical fixed-width CalVer.** `ParseCalVer` is now EXTREMELY STRICT with NO backward compatibility ‚Äî it accepts ONLY the canonical `YYYY.DDD.HHMM` form: exactly a 4-digit year, a 3-digit zero-padded day-of-year, and a 4-digit zero-padded HHMM, range-checked (day 1-366, hour 0-23, minute 0-59). A non-canonical value (legacy `4`, a non-padded `2026.45.830`) is "not a CalVer", which the load gate treats as older-than-HEAD so it flows into `charly migrate` and is re-stamped canonical ‚Äî one clean migration forward. `CalVer.String()`/`ComputeCalVerAt`/`pkg/arch/calver.sh` emit `%04d.%03d.%04d`; because every component is fixed-width, `CalVer.Less` is a plain string comparison and a `sort.Strings` of CalVer strings is chronological (`TestCalVerAlphanumericSort`). The per-push git tag formula simplified to `v$(date -u +%Y.%j.%H%M)` (`%j`/`%H%M` are already zero-padded ‚Äî Jan 1 @ 1 AM ‚Üí `v2026.001.0100`). Every CalVer literal in the registry + fixtures was normalized to canonical.

**Human/AI voice ‚Üí "you".** Per the project's two-tasters-at-one-bench tenet, the human‚Üîagent *actor* duality and agent-*audience* phrases across the docs were collapsed to "you" / "you and your agents" (e.g. VISION "serves the human at the keyboard and the agent driving" ‚Üí "serves you at the keyboard and your agents driving"; jupyter "AI agents can create cells" ‚Üí "You can create cells"). Governance autonomy distinctions were preserved by re-expressing them on the attended/unattended axis, never erased (`disposable:` authorizes UNATTENDED autonomous rebuild; an explicit `charly update` is attended). Product/system/citation names were KEPT (AI iteration loop, AI runner/sandbox, AI gateway, AI CLIs, AI Attribution, the Fedora AI Contribution Policy), as were compound descriptors (human-readable, human-authored, the canonical "first human user" account). This supersedes the prior `2026-06-12` voice entry's note that `kind: ai` was kept.

Verified: `go test ./...` (incl. the new strict-CalVer / alphanumeric-sort / agent-rename tests), `task build:charly` (`charly version` ‚Üí canonical `2026.163.0758`), `charly box validate` (zero warnings ‚Äî the renamed `agent:` catalog classifies cleanly, the residual gate doesn't false-positive, the canonical stamp is accepted), the `agent-kind-rename` migration applied + idempotent on the repo's own `charly.yml`, and `charly eval run eval-local` PASS (steps=4) on a disposable bed (fresh build‚Üídeploy‚Üívalidate through the new loader). The box submodules are imported via pinned `@github` tags (auto-migrated on fetch), so they are out of this cutover; the live agent-grader CLI-spawn path is unit-tested + loader-validated (the live run is gated by the eval-sandbox host precondition). Landed across pkg/arch + plugins + the superproject.

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî fix(vm): `resolveVmBackend` spawns the session daemon before probing (socket-activation / on-demand autospawn detection)

`resolveVmBackend()` stat'd the libvirt session socket COLD ‚Äî before any daemon spawn ‚Äî so on hosts that ship no persistent `virtqemud.socket` (Arch / CachyOS, where the session socket exists only AFTER a client triggers libvirt's on-demand autospawn) a fully-working libvirt false-negatived and silently fell back to qemu (or errored on `backend: libvirt`). The bug was per-verb nondeterministic: only some call sites (`charly vm create`, the eval-bed runner) pre-spawned via `startLibvirtUserSession()`, so `charly vm build/start/stop/destroy/console` resolved the backend cold. Fix: `resolveVmBackend()` now calls the idempotent best-effort `startLibvirtUserSession()` ITSELF before the socket probe, so every verb detects libvirt uniformly. `startLibvirtUserSession` became a swappable package var so the hermetic `TestResolveVmBackend_*` tests (which point `XDG_RUNTIME_DIR` at a socket-less temp dir) stub the spawn to a no-op ‚Äî an un-stubbed real spawn was creating a socket inside the test's temp dir and defeating the "no socket present" fixture. The standing lesson, now in `/charly-vm:vm` + `/charly-eval:eval`: NEVER gauge libvirt availability with `systemctl is-active <virtqemud|libvirtd>.service` ‚Äî a socket-activated / autospawn daemon reports the SERVICE inactive while libvirt is fully usable; the socket (`$XDG_RUNTIME_DIR/libvirt/virtqemud-sock`) or a real `virsh -c qemu:///session list` is the only valid signal. The system/rootful `qemu:///system` daemon is separate; charly is rootless-first (`qemu:///session`). Surfaced when an AI session's own `systemctl --user is-active` probe false-negatived a working libvirt (`virsh -c qemu:///session` connected fine and listed a domain). Proven on the cold path (kill virtqemud ‚Üí a vm op respawns the socket) + `charly eval run eval-charly-vm`.

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî feat(validate)!: mandatory ADE description + eval on every candy

`charly box validate` now hard-errors when a LOCAL candy lacks a full ADE `description:` (non-empty `feature:` + ‚â•1 `scenario:`) OR a non-empty `eval:` list ‚Äî ADE acceptance coverage is mandatory per candy (the spec IS the test), flipping the prior OPT-IN posture. Implemented in `validateCandyContents` (reuses `ValidateDescription`; scoped to `!Remote`, same as the mandatory-`version:` rule); Go test fixtures stamp minimal ADE via the existing `vCandies` helper (the trick the mandatory-version cutover used). Every candy was authored compliant: 186 main-repo (4 already compliant; the bulk via an agent-fan-out workflow ‚Äî a 12-candy pilot then paced chunks of 8 after a 16-wide fan-out tripped a server rate-limit, the last 15 hand-authored after a monthly spend limit halted agents), 2 in box/arch, 8 in box/cachyos (the submodule candies landed in their own repos at v2026.163.0736). No schema-shape migration ‚Äî description/eval are existing fields, so there is nothing to convert; the validator hard-error + the `/charly-eval:eval` hint is the external-user UX (real content can't be auto-generated per R4/ADE). Policy flipped opt-in‚Üímandatory (R5): CLAUDE.md ADE section + "Tests ship with the image" Key Rule, the strict-policy / eval / validate skills, README. The enforcing validator caught + fixed one real defect (a multi-keyword Gherkin step in redis-server-layer). Proven via `charly eval run eval-local` (fresh-rebuild R10 of the validator + a changed candy's ADE runtime path) + enforced `charly box validate` green on all 3 repos; the broader candy set's composing pod / VM / GPU beds are hardware-gated and were not run (those edits are additive ADE metadata validated by the enforcing validate). Five-repo atomic landing: box/arch + box/cachyos (tagged) + plugins + pkg/arch first, then the superproject pointer bump (`v2026.163.0740`).

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî docs(policy): second-person voice ‚Äî rewrite "the AI" actor refs in CLAUDE.md to "you"

CLAUDE.md mixed third-person "the AI" actor references with the second-person voice it uses everywhere else (title "for You and Your Agents"). The three actor spots ‚Äî the Skill Dispatcher's "(image or deploy, AI or human)" deploy-config row, R2's escalation "a genuine crossroad the AI cannot resolve alone", and the Post-Execution "STARTING the next one is the AI's job ‚Ä¶ the AI automatically opens ‚Ä¶ ANY issue it has found ‚Ä¶ it cannot resolve" ‚Äî are rewritten to "you" / "your" (with the bound `it`/`its` pronouns swept). Proper-noun / technical uses of "AI" are deliberately KEPT (AI Attribution, AI-attribution trailer, AI benchmark, AI-agent scoring, `kind: ai`, Agent Driven Evaluation, the Fedora AI Contribution Policy). Docs-only, zero behavior change; landed as `v2026.163.0445`.

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî chore(hooks): commit/push gates block `core.hooksPath` overrides ‚Äî the config spelling of `--no-verify`

Follow-on cutover from the hooks-hardening adversarial review (the round-2 out-of-scope observation, operator-classified as worth its own cutover): `git -c core.hooksPath=/dev/null commit` bypasses the project's git hooks exactly as `--no-verify` does, yet sailed through both gates ‚Äî a deterministic gate that blocks one spelling of an invariant but not another is incomplete on its own claim. Both `pre-commit-gate.sh` and `pre-push-gate.sh` now block any `core.hookspath` mention (case-insensitive) in the matched invocation's GLOBAL-options span (between `git` and the subcommand, where the `-c key=value` form must live) ‚Äî by construction this leaves `git commit -c <commit>` (the reuse-message flag), commit messages mentioning the key, and innocent `-c` overrides (`user.email=‚Ä¶`) untouched. Env-var config injection (`GIT_CONFIG_*`) stays out of scope, stated honestly in both gate headers and the `/charly-internals:agents` enumeration: the gate is a discipline backstop, not a security boundary. CLAUDE.md's hooks-doctrine bullet names the new invariant ("hook bypass via `--no-verify` or a `core.hooksPath` override").

### 2026-06-12 ‚Äî chore(hooks)!: ultra-lean pointer hooks; pre-commit gate blocks `syntax check only` on commits; agents/skill staleness sync

The three reminder hooks had grown back into the "walls of text" the hooks doctrine forbids, with the same rule content restated across them (drift risk multiplied): R10 gate-by-class + attribution/no-inflation + the 2026-04-26 incident + the one-phase rule appeared in BOTH `runtime-verification-reminder.sh` (UserPromptSubmit) and `end-of-turn-challenge.sh` (Stop); RDD was restated in all three; `team-coordination-reminder.sh` restated ~40 lines of the `/charly-internals:agents` bed-scoped model. All three are now ULTRA-LEAN POINTERS (‚â§10 output lines each, operator-chosen depth): section-name pointers into CLAUDE.md / the owning skills plus at most ONE behavioral anchor each (the consult-order ‚âÝ truth-order line survives compressed in the prompt hook; "KEEP WORKING / one specific question" in the Stop hook; disjoint-bed ownership + lead-owns-the-commit in the team hook). Gate hardening: `pre-commit-gate.sh` drops `syntax check only` from the legal-on-commit tier set and blocks it with a dedicated message ‚Äî the CLAUDE.md AI-Attribution table already pairs that tier with "do NOT commit", making it an unambiguous mechanical invariant per the doctrine (legal on a commit now: `fully tested and validated`, `analysed on a live system`; docs-only cutovers ship at the former per the provision). The same pass closes the `-n` short-alias hole in the bypass check ‚Äî `git commit -n` (and bundled forms like `-an`/`-anm`; a bundled `-m` starts the message VALUE, so `-amnope`-style tokens never false-trigger) is `--no-verify` and now blocks, scanned pre-message only by design (message text cannot be parsed out of a raw command string); `git push -n` is dry-run and stays untouched, while the push gate's force check goes bundle-aware symmetrically (`-fu` now blocks). Two adversarial-review rounds drove the `/charly-internals:agents` gate enumeration to match gate behavior at its stated granularity (any tier outside the legal-on-commit set blocks, not just the two named ones; absent-trailer detection is inline-`-m`-only and scoped to the commit invocation's own arg span ‚Äî a foreign `-m` elsewhere on the line no longer false-triggers, and a `-F`/heredoc/command-substituted message is not scanned for absence; force-push blocking includes `-f`, bundled forms included). Both gate scripts gain the exec bit the reminder hooks already had. Plugins side: `/charly-internals:agents` "Hooks doctrine" gains the first complete 5-hook inventory table (file ‚Üí event ‚Üí role; `end-of-turn-challenge.sh` was previously named in no skill), its gate enumeration adds the new tier block, and the roster section states that an agent's narrowed `tools:` frontmatter is ROLE-lane discipline, never a security boundary (security lives at the candybox wall ‚Äî VISION tenet 1). Agent staleness: `layer-validator` invariant 2 named the composition-splicing field `layers` ‚Äî the loader field is `candy` (`charly/config.go` `yaml:"candy"`); `testing-validator` standard 7 ("Behavior matches CLAUDE.md documentation") now points at the owning skill per the five-way doc split. Audit results recorded for completeness: the 4 workflows' CLAUDE.md citations all resolve, `settings.json` hook wiring is complete and correct, and `root-cause-analyzer` / `eval-bed-runner` / `deploy-verifier` were found current ‚Äî no changes. Operational note: the Skill tool serves plugin skills from a snapshot taken at session start, so a session spanning a landing can see pre-landing skill text (observed here as already-fixed "CLAUDE.md Law N" citations resurfacing); the working tree is ground truth.

### 2026-06-11 ‚Äî fix(workflows): verify-status substrate map + Workflow-args decoding across all four workflows

Two live-proven defects: (1) the Workflow harness delivers tool-passed args as a JSON-encoded STRING (probed empirically: `typeof args === 'string'`, `"[\"local\"]"`), so every workflow's `Array.isArray(args)` normalization silently mis-parsed tool invocations ‚Äî `/verify-status local` ran ALL substrates (its lenient discover agent fanned out over an empty map) and `/verify-beds eval-local` only worked because its discover agent happened to decode the JSON-ish token; (2) verify-status.js's SUBSTRATE_BEDS predated the box inversion (pod bed lives in `box/fedora`, android bed + its split `status-shows-android`/`status-shows-nested` checks in `box/cachyos`) and the script ran whatever the discover agent returned instead of intersecting with the selected map. Fixes: a shared JSON-decode-first args normalization in all four workflows (verify-beds, verify-status, audit-deploy-configs, triage-eval-failure); dir-aware bed runs (`charly -C box/<distro> eval run <bed>` + `<dir>/.eval/‚Ä¶`) in verify-beds + verify-status; verify-status's map corrected (real bed homes, multi-check android) with a strict confirm-only discover prompt and an authoritative code-side intersection so an over-helpful agent can narrow but never widen the run set. Gate: `/verify-status local` ran EXACTLY eval-local (PASS, verbatim status-shows-local assertion) and `/verify-beds eval-local` PASS (steps=4) through the changed scripts; all four parse.

### 2026-06-11 ‚Äî fix(eval): fail fast when a score's pod target has no deploy entry on this host

`charly eval run <score>` restarts-but-never-creates its sandbox pod by design, but a host without the operator-provisioned `eval-sandbox` deploy entry surfaced the gap as podman's raw `no container with name or ID "charly-eval-sandbox"` exit-125 ‚Äî the silent `cfg.Deploy[tn]` preflight skip hid the missing precondition (RCA'd live on this host, which has never carried the entry). The pod dispatch now resolves the entry through `scorePodTargetEntry` and errors actionably ‚Äî `score X targets pod Y but no deploy entry exists on this host ‚Äî provision the harness sandbox first: charly deploy add Y <ref> --disposable ‚Ä¶` ‚Äî and a per-host overlay load failure surfaces instead of being swallowed. Go tests cover the nil-config / missing-entry / present-entry branches; `/charly-eval:eval` now documents the sandbox as an operator-provisioned per-host precondition.

### 2026-06-11 ‚Äî fix(build): derive `task build:charly`'s package-displace list from the PKGBUILD (no more drift)

`task build:charly` failed on any host with the pre-rename `overthink-git` package installed: `opencharly-git and overthink-git are in conflict ‚Ä¶ unresolvable package conflicts`. The PKGBUILD correctly declares `conflicts=('overthink-git' 'ov-git')` + `replaces=('overthink-git' 'ov-git')`, but `pacman -U` (what `makepkg -i` runs for a local-file install) does NOT honor `replaces=`, so the Taskfile pre-removes the superseded packages first ‚Äî and its hardcoded list (`ov-git ov-git-debug opencharly-git opencharly-git-debug`) had drifted from the PKGBUILD, omitting `overthink-git`/`overthink-git-debug` (its comment even mis-cited `replaces=('opencharly-git' 'ov-git')`). The classic two-sources-of-truth drift. Fixed by DERIVING the displace-list from the PKGBUILD's own `conflicts=`/`replaces=` arrays (`bash -c 'source ./PKGBUILD ‚Ä¶'`) plus each entry's `-debug` sibling and the package's own `-debug` sibling ‚Äî so the list can never drift from the PKGBUILD again. R10: `task build:charly` on this host (with `overthink-git` installed) removed it and installed `opencharly-git` system-wide, EXIT 0.

### 2026-06-11 ‚Äî feat(generate)!: `charly box generate <name>` + `all` default, unified with build selection, and DETERMINISTIC auto-intermediates

`charly box generate` gained the box selection surface `charly box build` already had, and the underlying auto-intermediate computation was made fully deterministic so generation is reproducible and maximizes build-cache reuse.

- **`charly box generate [<box>‚Ä¶]`** ‚Äî new optional positional. `generate <name>` scopes emission to that box + its transitive deps (Base + format builders + bootstrap builder); `generate all` and bare `generate` emit every enabled box (the sentinel `all` is case-insensitive and collapses to the no-arg form). Adds `--include-disabled` (scoped to the named boxes), mirroring `charly box build`.
- **Unified build/generate selection (R3).** Two shared helpers ‚Äî `normalizeBoxArgs` (collapses the `all` sentinel to nil) and `boxResolveOpts` (empty ‚Üí all enabled; named ‚Üí `RequestedBoxes` scoping + per-name `--include-disabled` gate relaxation) ‚Äî are the single source of the selection rule for BOTH verbs. `BuildCmd.Run` normalizes `all` at the top (before remote-ref dispatch / include-passthrough so `all` is never mistaken for a remote target) and `Generate()` scopes its emission loop through the SAME `filterBox` the build path uses. Net effect: `charly box build <name>` now also generates only `<name>` + deps instead of all-then-filter ‚Äî fewer `.build/` writes, less cross-image churn.
- **Deterministic auto-intermediates.** `GlobalCandyOrder` and `ComputeIntermediates` iterated Go maps whose randomized order leaked into (a) authored-list cycle-skipping edge insertion, (b) sibling-group processing order ‚Üí `pickAutoName`'s `-2`/`-3` collision suffix, and (c) `collectSubtreeBoxes` ‚Üí the intermediate's format/distro union order. Result: bare `charly box generate` produced a *different* set of auto-intermediate images run-to-run (observed 46/49/48 boxes in box/fedora), and a box that intermittently vanished from the requestable set ("unknown box fedora"). Fixed by sorting every order-affecting map iteration (box names, candy names, a new `sortedSiblingKeys` by (base, uid), and `sortedKeys` in subtree collection). Now generation is byte-identical across runs AND a single-box generation emits byte-identical Containerfiles (intermediates included) to the full build ‚Äî so a box built in isolation reuses the full build's cache (matching FROM SHAs). Verified: box/fedora 8√ó identical + single==all across 5 targets (0 mismatches); box/cachyos 4√ó identical + single==all across selkies-labwc/openclaw-desktop/versa.
- **Coverage.** `box_selection_test.go` (selection logic + Kong parse) and `intermediates_determinism_test.go` (50-trial determinism on a fixture that reproduces all three non-determinism sources ‚Äî proven to FAIL with the fix reverted). R10: `charly eval run eval-pod` (disposable) PASS (steps=10), the build leg exercising scoped generate + deterministic intermediates on a fresh rebuild.
